# Puheo Improvements вҖ” Autonomous Pass

Running ledger. One line per shipped improvement, newest at the bottom of each section.

- [2026-04-27 L1] [UI/UX] Replaced eight decorative emoji spans in app.html (mode-icon Г—5, path-mixed-icon, mastery-intro-icon, scaffold-fire) with inline Lucide SVG and an `.icon-lucide` base class вҖ” finishes the deferred restraint-pass icon swap.
- [2026-04-27 L2] [Feature] Animated streak flame on dashboard rail вҖ” dim/warm/hot/inferno tiers (1d, 7d, 30d) with subtle flicker keyframes, prefers-reduced-motion safe; corrected latent bug where `dash-streak` was losing its `.mono-num` class on render.
- [2026-04-27 L3] [Feature] "Sana pГӨivГӨssГӨ" rail card вҖ” 50 curated B1вҖ“B2 YO-themed Spanish words (verb, adj., subst., ilmaus) with Spanish + Finnish example pair, deterministic UTC-day rotation so all users see the same word per day.
- [2026-04-27 L4] [Feature] Writing autosave + draft restore вҖ” debounced autosave to localStorage on every keystroke, prompt-matched restore (24 h TTL) with visible "Tallennettu klo HH.MM" / "вҶ© Palautettu kesken jГӨГӨnyt vastaus" indicator above the submit button.
- [2026-04-27 L5] [Feature] Spanish pronunciation buttons via Web Speech API on vocab `meaning`/`context` questions and gap-fill sentences вҖ” picks the best es-* voice, pulses while speaking, gracefully hides when speechSynthesis is unsupported.
- [2026-04-27 L6] [AI] Sharpened YTL writing grading prompt: explicit edge-case handling (empty / wrong-language / off-topic responses), error excerpts must be the SHORTEST span, error explanations must reference the rule (teach why), new `next_action_fi` field giving one concrete next step anchored to the weakest dimension; rendered as a highlighted "Seuraava askel" card on the feedback screen.
- [2026-04-27 L7] [Feature] Daily challenge card on dashboard вҖ” 25 curated rotating micro-missions across vocab/grammar/reading/writing, deterministic UTC-day rotation, "Aloita haaste вҶ’" deep-links to the matching mode, "Ohita tГӨnГӨГӨn" persists in localStorage so the card hides for the rest of the day.
- [2026-04-27 L8] [UI/UX] Tactile answer-feedback animations вҖ” correct = subtle bounce + soft green ring pulse; wrong = quick horizontal shake. Applied to both `.ex-option` (vocab/grammar MC) and `.gap-fill-input`; both gated by `prefers-reduced-motion: reduce`.
- [2026-04-27 L9] [UI/UX] Time-aware Finnish dashboard greeting вҖ” "Huomenta / PГӨivГӨГӨ / Iltaa, [name]." swapped at 5/11/17/23 h boundaries (defaults to "Hei" outside the named windows).
- [2026-04-27 L10] [UI/UX] Variable contextual motivation copy on dashboard вҖ” six buckets (zero / zero-streak / 1-2d / 3-6d / 7-13d / 14-29d / 30d+) with 3-4 lines each, deterministic UTC-day rotation so the same line never repeats two days running.
- [2026-04-27 L11] [Infra] SW cache `puheo-v49 вҶ’ puheo-v50` and added new feature modules (`wordOfDay.js`, `dailyChallenge.js`, `speak.js`) to STATIC_ASSETS so they precache on install.

Reduced `.section` padding to `56 px 20 px` (mobile) / `64 px 20 px` (вүҘ960 px). Trimmed the floating exercise-card mockup wrapper bottom padding from 60вҶ’32 px. - [2026-04-27 L15] [Perf] **CLS 0.163 вҶ’ 0.000, app.html performance 85 вҶ’ 93.** Re-ran Lighthouse and used `audits["layout-shifts"]` to confirm the single-largest shift was on `<div id="screen-auth">` itself: the initial HTML paints with the 3-column app-shell grid (sidebar + main + rail) and the auth screen inside the squished middle column; then `js/ui/nav.js` fires `applyShellMode("screen-auth")` after DOMContentLoaded, adds `body.auth-mode`, and the grid collapses to 1-column вҖ” that re-flow is the entire CLS budget. Fix: a 7-line inline `<script>` immediately after `<body>` reads `localStorage.puheo_token` and synchronously adds `body.auth-mode` before first paint when no token is present. The CSS path then matches first paint, no re-flow. Logged-in users keep the 3-col layout because the script doesn't add the class. Bumped SW cache `puheo-v64 вҶ’ puheo-v65`. Skill: ui-ux-pro-max P3 performance (CLS clean budget), P4 layout (no token-presence guesswork at the CSS layer); `puheo-screen-template` (the 8 px-grid spacing pattern stays untouched, this is purely a paint-order fix).

- [2026-04-27 L16] [AI] First application of the `puheo-ai-prompt` skill. Audited `lib/writingGrading.js` against the skill spec вҖ” already strong (YO-koe lyhyt framing, dimension rubric anchors, edge-case handling for empty/wrong-language/off-topic, shortest-span error excerpts, rule-anchored Finnish explanations, server-side total/band recompute, guardrails) вҖ” so the prompt itself didn't need a rewrite this loop. The gap was at the call layer: `callOpenAI()` was passing only `model`, `max_tokens`, `messages` вҖ” no `response_format` (so the model's JSON would occasionally be wrapped in `\`\`\`json` fences, requiring a regex strip) and no `temperature` (so every grader call defaulted to 0.7, which is generation-grade nondeterminism). Two changes: (1) `callOpenAI(prompt, maxTokens, opts)` now passes `opts.temperature` and `opts.responseFormat` to the OpenAI body when set, default behavior unchanged; (2) `routes/writing.js` grader call passes `{ temperature: 0.2, responseFormat: { type: "json_object" } }`. Two students with identical text now get a much more consistent grade, and the JSON parse no longer fails when the model wraps in markdown. Generators (vocab/grammar/reading) keep the existing default 0.7 / no response_format. Skills applied: `puheo-ai-prompt` rules #2 (structured output) + #8 (cost guards: deterministic temperature for graders); ui-ux-pro-max P3 performance (one fewer regex-strip per grade response).

- [2026-04-27 L17] [AI] Made JSON-mode the default in `callOpenAI()`. Every Puheo route today asks the model to emit JSON; ~17 callsites across `routes/{adaptive,exam,exercises,writing}.js`. Without `response_format: { type: "json_object" }` the model occasionally wraps in markdown fences and the downstream regex-strip + JSON.parse fallback chain has to clean up. Default it, allow opt-out via `opts.responseFormat: null` for the rare plain-text case (none today). All 17 generators and graders now benefit immediately вҖ” fewer parse retries, fewer cache-poisoning fragments, more deterministic responses. Only one downstream change needed: the writing grader (L16) which already passes `temperature: 0.2 + responseFormat: { type: "json_object" }` continues to work because `opts.responseFormat || { type: "json_object" }` resolves to its explicit value when set. Skill applied: `puheo-ai-prompt` rule #2 (structured output, default-on across the project), rule #9 (server-side JSON validation pipeline shortened by one defensive layer).

## Snapshot at loop 10

**Total loops shipped this pass: 11** (L0 + L0.5 Г—3 + L1..L10).

**Biggest 3 wins:**
1. **Accessibility 28 axe violations вҶ’ 0** and **app console errors 69 вҶ’ 0** through L0..L6. Lighthouse a11y score: **100/100** on both landing and app.html. The user's "lots of bugs" verdict was largely a11y debt; that debt is paid.
2. **Visual identity ladder shipped end-to-end** вҖ” auth screen now has a dark-teal value-prop panel (L8), exercise screen sits in a contained card with shadow instead of floating in green void (L5), results screens have hero-score + Oikein/VГӨГӨrin/Aika stats strip + confetti for вүҘ80% (L4), each mode-page has its own color identity (L9). The full first-session flow (auth вҶ’ dashboard вҶ’ exercise вҶ’ results) reads as a designed product, not a school project.
3. **Voice + empty-state foundation** вҖ” three Puheo skills shipped at L0.5 (`puheo-screen-template`, `puheo-finnish-voice`, `puheo-ai-prompt`); every visible string passes the encouraging-not-condescending bar; loading states are Finnish ("EtsitГӨГӨn tehtГӨvГӨГӨвҖҰ") with shimmer; empty states are coach cards with illustration + headline + body + CTA, not "Ei tietoja."

**Anything risky to QA before deploy:**
- The L0 + L3 helmet CSP edits (`eu-assets.i.posthog.com`, `fonts.googleapis.com`, `fonts.gstatic.com` in connect-src) only take effect on a server restart. The lingering 6 landing console errors are all the same posthog 401 + 404 from this вҖ” should clear on restart.
- The exercise-screen card containment in `css/components/exercise.css` uses `#screen-exercise > .exercise` (and similar) selectors at `min-width: 769 px`. Mobile is unaffected. Verify on a real desktop browser that the card border + shadow show up вҖ” at 1440 px the screenshot confirms it, but Safari + Firefox should be sanity-checked.
- The auth screen 2-column layout (L8) appears at вүҘ960 px. At exactly 960 px the gradient panel suddenly appears вҖ” verify there's no awkward layout flash for users right at that boundary.
- `canvas-confetti@1.9.4` was vendored to `js/vendor/confetti.mjs` (24 KB ESM). Production deploy should serve it. The lazy-import is `import("../vendor/confetti.mjs")` вҖ” relative path, needs the file present.
- SW cache bumped many times (v50 вҶ’ v60). First deploy after this batch will refetch every STATIC_ASSET on every active client. Heads-up.

- [2026-04-27 L8] [UI/UX] Closed P1-9 (auth screen looked incomplete with sidebar absent). Wrapped `#screen-auth` in a new `.auth-shell` 2-column grid; at вүҘ960 px shows a left-side `.auth-aside` value-prop panel and the existing form on the right; below 960 px the aside is hidden and the form keeps its current single-column layout (mobile unaffected). ## Summary

**Total improvements shipped:** 11 loops across UI/UX (5), Feature (4), AI (1), Infra (1).

**Top 3:**

1. **L6 вҖ” sharpened YTL writing grading prompt with `next_action_fi`.** The biggest pedagogical lift: edge-case handling for empty / wrong-language / off-topic submissions, error explanations that must reference the rule (teach why, not just what), and a dedicated "Seuraava askel" card that gives the student exactly one concrete next move anchored to their weakest dimension.
2. **L5 вҖ” Web Speech API pronunciation on vocab + gap-fill.** Genuinely useful, zero new dependencies, picks the best available es-* voice, gracefully hides on browsers without `speechSynthesis`. A single click and a Finnish student hears how `el medio ambiente` is actually pronounced.
3. **L1 вҖ” full Lucide SVG sweep in `app.html`.** Closes the deferred restraint-pass item that was just hiding decorative emoji via CSS. Eight icons swapped to inline Lucide strokes with an `.icon-lucide` base class so they pick up font-size + currentColor automatically.

**Manual QA risks before deploy:**
- Web Speech API: tested logic-only вҖ” verify on Safari and Firefox that `speakSpanish` actually plays (Firefox in particular has flaky es-* voice support; the button should hide if no voice is found, but watch for a click that produces silence on first load before voices populate).
- Writing autosave: restore-on-load needs a real browser test вҖ” confirm that closing and re-opening the writing screen with the same prompt actually refills the textarea and the indicator says "вҶ© Palautettu kesken jГӨГӨnyt vastaus".
- SW cache jumped v48 вҶ’ v50; first deploy will refetch every STATIC_ASSET. Watch for any 404 on the three newly-listed modules вҖ” check that `/js/features/{wordOfDay,dailyChallenge,speak}.js` actually serves from the production hosting.

**5 highest-value follow-ups (with another 2 h):**
1. **Speech recognition for pronunciation practice** вҖ” pair with the existing speaker buttons; webkit/standard `SpeechRecognition`, fuzzy-match transcript against expected text, show "вң“ Hyvin sanottu / вң— YritГӨ uudelleen вҖ” kuulin '...'".
2. **XP + level system, persisted server-side** вҖ” adds a real progress loop on top of streaks; needs Supabase `xp` column + dashboard XP bar with level threshold copy.
3. **Cross-batch vocab variety** вҖ” pass recently-shown headwords from the client to `routes/exercises.js` and forbid them in the prompt; would noticeably reduce the repeat-word feel on long sessions.
4. **Achievement system** вҖ” small Supabase table (`achievements_unlocked`) + dashboard rail card "5 / 12 saavutusta avattu" with the next-to-unlock teased; reuses the streak/heatmap data we already collect.
5. **Shareable score card (canvas image)** вҖ” on writing feedback, "Jaa вҶ’" generates a 1080Г—1350 PNG with the YTL grade, dimension scores, and one positive annotation; downloadable, instagrammable. Pure frontend canvas, no extra deps.

- [2026-04-28 L18] [AI] Cross-batch vocab anti-repetition. Long sessions made it feel like the same Spanish words came back every batch (skill `puheo-ai-prompt` rule #4, idea-well item #3). Plumbed a `recentlyShown: string[]` field through `js/screens/vocab.js вҶ’ /api/generate вҶ’ routes/exercises.js вҶ’ OpenAI prompt`. After each batch the client extracts a Spanish-lemma key from each exercise (`extractClientHeadwordKey`, mirrors the existing server `extractHeadwordKey` heuristic вҖ” strips `A) ` prefix and articles `el/la/un/una/...`), accumulates into `state.recentVocabHeadwords`, capped at the most recent 30 entries. The server sanitises (array of lowercase strings, вүӨ40 chars, вүӨ30 entries) and, when non-empty, appends a single Finnish-friendly anti-repetition instruction to the prompt: "ANTI-REPETITION: the student has already seen these target headwords this session вҖ” do NOT use any of them as a target word in this batch (variation in options is fine, but pick fresh target lemmas): word1, word2, ...". Empty list path is identical to before, so safe. Reset on `btn-restart`. SW v65 вҶ’ v66. Bank exercises already de-dup via `seen_exercises` (30-day window); the new logic targets the AI-generated freshness path which is where repeats were visible. Skills applied: `puheo-ai-prompt` rule #4 (anti-repetition guidance baked into the prompt), rule #7 (sanitise variable user input before injecting into prompts).

- [2026-04-28 L19] [AI] Mirrored L18 anti-repetition pattern to grammar drills. The `/grammar-drill` prompt already says "topic=mixed вҶ’ cover at least 3 distinct rules per batch", but that constraint only applied within a batch вҖ” across batches the model could (and did) keep cycling the same handful of rules. Same plumbing as L18 but keyed on the natural grammar identifier `rule` (e.g. "ser/estar", "imperfekti", "ojalГЎ+subj.") rather than the lemma key used for vocab. Client (`js/screens/grammar.js`): sends `recentlyShown: state.recentGrammarRules` ONLY when `state.grammarTopic === "mixed"` вҖ” when the student explicitly picked a single rule we WANT every batch to keep drilling it, so the gate is correct. After each response, lowercase rule labels are accumulated into `state.recentGrammarRules` capped at 20. State (`js/state.js`): new field `recentGrammarRules: []`. Server (`routes/exercises.js` `/grammar-drill`): accepts `recentlyShown`, sanitises (lowercase strings, вүӨ40 chars, вүӨ20 entries), and when `topic === "mixed"` AND list non-empty appends an "ANTI-REPETITION" rule to the prompt that asks the model to prefer DIFFERENT rules in this batch. Empty-list path is identical to pre-L19. SW v66 вҶ’ v67. `node --check` passes on all three changed JS files. Skills applied: `puheo-ai-prompt` rule #4 (anti-repetition baked into the prompt), rule #7 (sanitise variable user input), rule #6 (gate prompt extensions on a meaningful state condition rather than always-on).

- [2026-04-28 L23] [UI/UX] Daily challenge вҖ” completion state (a "done today" celebratory variant). The dashboard already rendered a daily challenge card (`js/features/dailyChallenge.js` is wired into `loadDashboard` via `renderDailyChallengeInto`), but the only state transitions were "show" and "skip today". A student who clicked "Aloita haaste вҶ’", went into vocab/grammar/reading/writing, finished the session, and came back to the dashboard would still see the same prompt вҖ” completely missing the dopamine of "вң“ done". Added: `markModeCompletedToday(mode)` in `dailyChallenge.js` reads today's challenge mode from the deterministic UTC-day rotation and only flips `localStorage.puheo_dailychallenge_done = day_number` when the just-completed mode matches. `dashboard.saveProgress` now calls `markModeCompletedToday(mode)` BEFORE the network call so the done state survives offline / unauthenticated finish-paths (the user did the work, the celebration should not depend on the API succeeding). `renderDailyChallengeInto` checks `isDoneToday()` first; if true, replaces the `actions` row with a green-tinted variant: kicker still says "TГӨnГӨГӨn В· haaste", title unchanged, body is "вң“ Hyvin meni вҖ” pГӨivГӨn haaste tehty. Theme-token-only (no hardcoded color), so dark mode just works once L11's `data-theme="dark"` tokens are applied. SW v70 вҶ’ v71. `node --check` clean. Skills: `puheo-finnish-voice` (encouraging "Hyvin meni вҖ” pГӨivГӨn haaste tehty. - [2026-04-28 L29] [UI/UX] YO-valmius readiness ring on the right rail. The rail stat used to be a flat `0%` text вҖ” competent but the most goal-oriented metric in the app deserved more presence. Sourced from Magic UI `animated-circular-progress-bar.tsx` (github.com/magicuidesign/magicui вҖ” apps/www/registry/magicui/animated-circular-progress-bar.tsx); ported to vanilla SVG. Markup: `<svg viewBox="0 0 80 80">` with two `<circle r="34">` вҖ” track via `var(--surface-2)` stroke, fill via `var(--accent)` stroke with `stroke-dasharray: 213.628; stroke-dashoffset: 213.628;` (213.628 = 2ПҖ Г— 34, rounded to a literal so the arc snaps without sub-pixel jitter). - [2026-04-28 L30] [UI/UX] "Kehitys ajan mittaan" chart polish вҖ” sourced from shadcn/ui line chart aesthetic. The hand-rolled SVG in `renderProgressChart` worked but used hardcoded `#e63946` (red) and `#f59e0b` (amber) literals, a sharp polyline (not curved), and per-point dots вҖ” visually plain and locked into one theme. Sourced shadcn `chart-line-default.tsx` (github.com/shadcn-ui/ui вҖ” apps/v4/registry/new-york-v4/charts/chart-line-default.tsx) for the visual language: `<CartesianGrid vertical={false}>` (horizontal-only grid), `<XAxis tickLine={false} axisLine={false}>` (no axis lines), `<Line type="natural" dot={false}>` (smooth Catmull-Rom curve, no per-point dots). Adapted: ported the natural-cubic-spline interpolation by hand (Catmull-Rom вҶ’ cubic-Bezier conversion: `C1 = P1 + (P2-P0)/6`, `C2 = P2 - (P3-P1)/6`, with endpoints duplicated as missing controls) so the line flows smoothly between points instead of zig-zagging. All hardcoded colors swapped to `var(--accent)` for stroke/fill + `currentColor` on grid/axis with an SVG-level `style="color: var(--ink-faint)"` so light/dark mode flips for free. Area fill below the curve uses the same Catmull-Rom path closed back to the baseline, with a `stop-color="var(--accent)"` 0.22вҶ’0 gradient. Removed the dashed amber "tГӨnГӨГӨn" vertical line вҖ” shadcn-style charts don't carry that sort of cursor decoration; the endpoint is implied by the bullseye dot. Endpoint dot is now a 3-layer "bullseye" (6r halo at 18% opacity + 3.5r solid accent + 1.4r surface-color inner punch) вҖ” same technique shadcn uses to make the latest data point visually punctual. Removed the per-point intermediate dots entirely вҖ” the line itself + the endpoint is enough. Verified with a 14-point grade series (B вҶ’ C вҶ’ вҖҰ вҶ’ L) at 1440 via `scripts/agent-test/loop30-chart-polish.mjs` вҖ” `loop-30-chart-clip.png` shows the smooth teal sweep with grade ladder labels and the bullseye landing on L. SW v78 вҶ’ v79. Sources: shadcn chart-line-default (visual language), Catmull-Rom-to-Bezier algorithm (standard mathematical conversion). Skills: ui-ux-pro-max P1 (proper chart hierarchy вҖ” line dominates, grid recedes, label is light), P2 (token-only via accent + currentColor вҖ” dark mode works automatically), P5 (no animation here вҖ” the chart is read on landing, not on transition; shadcn similarly keeps line charts static).

- [2026-04-28 L37] [BUG] Settings page Muokkaa buttons all dead вҖ” root cause was a CSS stacking-context issue. The settings buttons rendered correctly and the click handlers were correctly wired in `js/screens/settings.js renderRows()`, but real-mouse clicks (verified via `page.mouse.click(x,y)` and `document.elementFromPoint(916, 52)`) hit-tested through to `<main id="app-main">` instead of the button. Reproduced via `scripts/agent-test/loop37e-real-mouse.mjs`: click target=`MAIN#app-main`, modal stays hidden. Diagnosis: `.app-main` has `position: relative; z-index: 1` (creates stacking context A). Inside A, `.app-main-inner` is in-flow (paint layer 3 of A). `.screen.active` is `position: absolute; inset: 0; z-index: auto` (paint layer 6 of A вҖ” positioned descendant with z-index auto). The static button descendants of `.screen` paint within layer 6 atomically вҖ” but with z-index auto, the screen does NOT establish its own stacking context, so its descendants share the parent context's depth resolution. Real browsers' hit-testing under this exact configuration ('parent has z-index, child positioned with z-index auto, grandchild static') resolves the topmost element at the click point as the parent (`<main>`) вҖ” verified empirically. **Fix:** added `z-index: 1; isolation: isolate;` to `.screen.active` in `style.css:354` so the active screen establishes a clean stacking context above `.app-main-inner`. First tried `position: relative; z-index: 1` (style.css:354) вҖ” broke the layout because static positioning made the screen flow below the countdown; reverted. Final fix preserves `position: absolute` and adds isolation. Verified end-to-end via `scripts/agent-test/loop37f-all-fields.mjs`: all 8 settings fields (exam_date, spanish_courses_completed, spanish_grade_average, study_background, weak_areas, strong_areas, preferred_session_length, target_grade) open the correct modal with the correct title and option count when clicked at their viewport coordinates. Profile screen regression-checked by re-running `loop36-profile-blur-fade.mjs` вҖ” passes. SW v85 вҶ’ v86. Sources: empirical Playwright `page.mouse.click()` + `document.elementFromPoint()` to confirm the actual hit target before fixing вҖ” the diagnostic technique itself is the takeaway: when the user reports "click does nothing" but the JS handler looks correct, hit-test the coords with a real browser, never trust `btn.click()` (programmatic) which bypasses hit-testing. Skills: superpowers:systematic-debugging (root-cause not symptom вҖ” verified via 5 successive Playwright probes before applying fix), verification-before-completion (real-mouse click + 8-field smoke + profile regression run before claiming done). New diagnostic scripts: `loop37-settings-repro.mjs`, `loop37b-settings-via-nav.mjs`, `loop37c-deep-probe.mjs`, `loop37d-find-blocker.mjs`, `loop37e-real-mouse.mjs`, `loop37f-all-fields.mjs`. PLAN.md item 1 of 7 complete; next loop = bug 2 (YO-readiness math).

- [2026-04-28 L38] [BUG] YO-valmius readiness math wrong вҖ” two compounding bugs in `js/features/writingProgression.js computeReadinessMap`. **Bug A (scale mismatch):** path-node `bestPct` arrives as a 0вҖ“1 fraction from `/api/learning-path` (`lib/learningPath.js:142` reads `row?.best_pct` which is normalised 0..1 in `routes/profile.js:204`). The frontend then computed `pct = Math.round((t.bestPct || 0) * 100) / 100` which divides by 100 a SECOND time вҖ” leaving `pct` still in 0..1 вҖ” and compared against `60 / 30 / 10` thresholds clearly intended as percent. Result: every in-progress topic stayed at level 0 regardless of best score. **Bug B (formula intent):** `readinessPct = mastered / total` where mastered = levelвүҘ3. Treats partial progress as zero вҖ” eight sessions touching eight topics at 30вҖ“50 % best read as "0 mastered" and the lone writing dim that hit avg 3 dragged the rail to "2 / 14 = 14 %". The user reported "8 harjoitusta = 14% YO-valmius" and flagged it as wrong-feeling; correct interpretation = "I've started everything but completed nothing yet". **Fix A:** dropped the redundant `/100` so `pct = Math.round((t.bestPct || 0) * 100)` lands in 0..100 to match the 60/30/10 thresholds. **Fix B:** replaced the binary mastered/total ratio with weighted partial credit вҖ” `readinessPct = round(sum(level) / (totalCells * 4) * 100)` вҖ” so each cell contributes its level/4 of full credit. Sanity-check via Node REPL on a representative payload (10 path nodes: 2 at bestPct 0.65, 3 at 0.35, 5 untouched + 4 writing dims at avg ~2.4): old formula вҶ’ 14 %, new formula вҶ’ 36 % вҖ” matches the user's mental model "I've done some work, I'm partway to ready". Edge cases verified: brand-new user (all status:available, bestPct 0, no writing data) вҶ’ 0 %; power user (8 mastered + 6 in-progress at 0.7 + 4 writing dims at avg 4.2) вҶ’ 96 %. Existing dashboard ring test (`scripts/agent-test/loop29-readiness-ring.mjs`) re-runs cleanly: ring state shows num=45 with matching dashoffset on a payload that previously showed 21 %. SW v86 вҶ’ v87 (writingProgression.js is in STATIC_ASSETS, so a bump is required to re-serve the patched file). Skills: superpowers:systematic-debugging (traced bestPct end-to-end through DB column вҶ’ API serializer вҶ’ frontend consumer rather than guessing the formula). PLAN.md item 2 of 7 complete; next loop = bug 3 (NaN pv sitten) + bug 4 (right sidebar overflow), bundled.

- [2026-04-28 L39] [BUG] NaN pv sitten + right-sidebar overflow вҖ” bundled bugs 3 + 4 from PLAN.md. **Bug 3 (NaN pv sitten):** `js/screens/dashboard.js timeAgo()` (line 382, pre-fix) had no null/NaN guard whatsoever вҖ” when `dateStr` was `undefined`, `new Date(undefined + "Z")` produced Invalid Date, `.getTime()` returned NaN, and the cascade-of-floor-and-compare fell through every threshold to land on `${days} pv sitten` with `days = NaN`. Profile.js had a defensive copy but with subtle holes (returned "" on NaN вҖ” silently dropping the row's time entirely, not great UX either). **Fix:** extracted a single shared, defensive helper `js/ui/timeAgo.js` that accepts ISO strings (with or without trailing Z), epoch numbers, and `Date` instances; falls back to "ГӨskettГӨin" (Finnish "recently") rather than ever emitting NaN; handles future timestamps the same way; rejects non-finite ms; adds a `kk вҶ’ v sitten` rollover at 12 months. Both `js/screens/dashboard.js` and `js/screens/profile.js` now import and use this single helper instead of carrying their own copies. Verified via Node REPL: null/undefined/empty вҶ’ ""; "not a date" вҶ’ "ГӨskettГӨin"; ISO with Z, ISO without Z, epoch ms, future Date all return the right Finnish phrase. **Bug 4 (right rail overflow):** could not reproduce overflow in any of 1180 / 1280 / 1440 / 1920 viewports via `scripts/agent-test/loop39-rail-overflow.mjs` and `loop39b-rail-deep.mjs` (which checks `scrollWidth > clientWidth` on every rail descendant вҖ” even after forcing the longest possible word-of-day text, no element overflowed). The user's report likely predated the L25 polish run. Applied a defensive belt-and-braces guard anyway: `.app-rail, .app-rail * { min-width: 0 }` + `overflow-wrap: anywhere; word-break: break-word` on `.word-of-day`, `.rail-stat__v`, `.rail-stat__l`, `.rail__h`. Long Spanish examples without spaces or unexpectedly long values can no longer push the column. Re-screenshotted at all four widths вҖ” clean. SW v87 вҶ’ v89 (added `/js/ui/timeAgo.js`, `/js/screens/settings.js`, `/js/screens/learningPath.js` to STATIC_ASSETS вҖ” settings + learningPath were silently missing despite being part of the SPA's screen graph). Files: NEW `js/ui/timeAgo.js`; edited `js/screens/dashboard.js`, `js/screens/profile.js`, `css/components/rail.css`, `sw.js`. Skills: superpowers:systematic-debugging (traced both bugs to root cause; could not reproduce bug 4 вҖ” applied defensive fix rather than fabricating a repro), verification-before-completion (Node REPL on every input shape + Playwright screenshot at four viewports). PLAN.md items 1-4 (all bugs) now complete in 3 ledger lines. **Next loops 40вҖ“42 = redesigns 5/6/7.** Per the user's brief these are big enough each warrants its own focused loop with fresh context вҖ” stopping here this session.

Inner `.cta-card__glow` is an absolutely-positioned radial-gradient `--accent-glow` blob blurred at 50 px so the title sits in a halo of mint, restrained-not-loud (opacity 0.55). Mobile breakpoint at 720 px collapses padding from `var(--sp-8) var(--sp-6)` вҶ’ `var(--sp-6) var(--sp-3)` and bumps radius down from `--r-xl` to `--r-lg` so the card doesn't feel oversized on a 375 px viewport. Footer: `background: var(--bg)` (explicit dark) so the section reads as outside the gradient'd content area; `border-top: 1px solid var(--border)` divides it from the CTA's accent-glow region. **A11y catch:** initial verifier pass had axe `color-contrast` (serious Г— 5) вҖ” `.landing-footer__col-title` and `.landing-footer__bottom` both used `--text-subtle: #71717a` against the explicit `var(--bg) #0a0a0a` footer background = 4.09:1, fails WCAG AA 4.5:1. Note: `--text-subtle` passes elsewhere on the page because `.hero` and most sections inherit the page's `--bg-gradient` (radial `#1a1a2e вҶ’ #0a0a0a 60%`) which lifts the bg toward `#1a1a2e` near the top of the viewport, but the explicit `var(--bg)` on the footer is pure `#0a0a0a` so the contrast drops below threshold. **Fix:** bumped `.landing-footer__col-title` and `.landing-footer__bottom` color to `var(--text-muted) #a1a1aa` = 9.7:1 against `#0a0a0a` (well above AAA), and bumped the inner `<time>` to `var(--text)` for max emphasis on the exam date. Same fix pattern as L43's `.browser-frame__url` bump (`--text-subtle` вҶ’ `--text-muted` on dark elevated surfaces). After fix: axe-core 4.10.2 across the entire page (now hero + problem + pillars + steps + grader + pricing + FAQ + CTA + footer): **0 violations** at 1440 + 375. **Verified** via `scripts/agent-test/loop48-cta-footer.mjs` (NEW, clone of L47 harness). Read screenshots both viewports: desktop CTA card sits as a glow-bordered closer with the mint button centred and the mint-glow bloom subtle behind the title; desktop footer reads as a clean 3-col sitemap with the brand left and the bottom row spanning both halves; mobile CTA collapses gracefully (title two-line balanced, button widens, fineprint wraps to 2 lines without overflow), mobile footer stacks brand-then-cols-then-bottom with no horizontal scroll at 375. - [2026-04-28 L47] [UI/UX] LANDING_PLAN.md Section C 8 вҖ” FAQ. Left column: 12 px `.faq__eyebrow` "UKK" in `--accent`, display H2 "Usein kysyttyГӨ Puheosta." with `text-wrap: balance`, 16 px muted `.faq__sub` with a `mailto:tuki@puheo.fi` link styled with mint underline-decoration so the support contact reads as the natural fallback path (not ALL-CAPS, not a button вҖ” restraint). Right column: 6 `<details class="faq-item" name="puheo-faq">` items separated by 1 px `--border` lines, top + bottom of list also bordered. The `name="puheo-faq"` attribute is the recent ExclusiveAccordion HTML primitive (Chrome 120+) вҖ” opens one item closes the others; gracefully no-op on older browsers (multiple-open is also valid behavior, not a bug). Each item: `<summary class="faq-item__q">` is a flexbox row with the question text on one side (display font, 18 px, weight 500, `--text` colour, `text-wrap: balance`) + an inline 18 px Lucide `chevron-right` SVG on the other, hover paints the row in `--accent`; `.faq-item__a` answer panel is a constrained-max-width 640 px column at `--text-muted` 16/1.6 line-height. Default disclosure markers killed across browsers via `summary { list-style: none }` + `::-webkit-details-marker { display: none }` + `::marker { content: "" }`. **Six honest answers** lifted verbatim from spec appendix #5 (sourced from `landing/DESIGN.md` В§10, marked reusable in L42's setup): (1) **YTL endorsement** вҖ” "Ei. YTL ei myГ¶nnГӨ yksittГӨisille palveluille hyvГӨksyntГ¶jГӨ, eikГӨ Puheo ole YTL:n tuottama tai vahvistama. Sen sijaan kirjoitusten arviointi on rakennettu suoraan YTL:n julkaiseman vieraan kielen lyhyen oppimГӨГӨrГӨn rubriikin pГӨГӨlle вҖҰ" вҖ” the most trust-buying answer in the doc per RESEARCH.md, leads the FAQ because honesty about endorsement matters more than every other claim. (2) **format-changes** вҖ” "Seuraamme YTL:n ohjeistusta ja pГӨivitГӨmme harjoitukset, rubriikin ja tehtГӨvГӨtyypit jokaisen julkaistun muutoksen jГӨlkeen. Pro-tilaajat saavat pГӨivitykset automaattisesti." (3) **GDPR/data** вҖ” "Vain rekisterГ¶itymiseen tarvittavat tiedot ja harjoitusdata вҖ” ei kolmansille osapuolille, ei mainostajille. Palvelu on GDPR-yhteensopiva ja kaikki data sГӨilytetГӨГӨn EU-alueella sijaitsevilla palvelimilla." (4) **mobile** вҖ” "KyllГӨ. Puheo on selainpohjainen ja toimii sellaisenaan iOS:n ja Androidin kosketusnГӨytГ¶illГӨ. Voit halutessasi lisГӨtГӨ Puheon kotinГӨytГ¶lle PWA:na вҖ” silloin se aukeaa kuin sovellus, ilman erillistГӨ asennusta." (5) **AI vs teacher** вҖ” "Kolme asiaa, joita tekoГӨly tekee paremmin kuin yksin opiskelu kirjan kanssa: arvioi kirjoituksesi 30 sekunnissa, muistaa tarkalleen mitkГӨ sanat ja rakenteet sinun on aika kerrata, ja on kГӨytettГӨvissГӨ silloin kun harjoittelet вҖ” klo 22:30 tai sunnuntai-iltapГӨivГӨnГӨ. HyvГӨ opettaja antaa muuta arvokasta вҖ” Puheo on harjoittelukumppani niiden tuntien vГӨlissГӨ, ei opettajan korvaaja." (6) **cancellation** вҖ” "Voit peruuttaa Pro-tilauksen sisГӨГӨnkirjautuneena yhdellГӨ klikkauksella, ja tilaus pГӨГӨttyy kuluvan laskutusjakson loppuun. Kertaostoille (esim. kesГӨpaketti) myГ¶nnГӨmme 14 pГӨivГӨn rahat-takaisin-takuun ilman erillistГӨ perustelua." Did **NOT** reuse the "10 vuoden YO-arkisto" claim вҖ” `landing/AUDIT.md` flagged it as un-defensible. **CSS port** (+115 lines into `css/landing.css`): all token-only вҖ” `--surface`, `--border`, `--accent`, `--text-muted`, `--r-pill`, `--sp-*`, `--fs-*`. Chevron rotation uses a `transform: rotate(0)` вҶ’ `rotate(90deg)` on `.faq-item[open] > .faq-item__q .faq-item__chev` with `transition: transform var(--t-mid)` (220 ms ease-out from the token sheet) + `color: --accent` swap; this animates everywhere (no feature gate). **Smooth height open** uses the modern `interpolate-size: allow-keywords` + `details::details-content` pseudo-element (Chrome 129+ / Edge 129+): `block-size: 0` + `opacity: 0` + `overflow: clip` at rest, `block-size: auto` + `opacity: 1` when `[open]`, with `transition: block-size var(--t-mid), opacity var(--t-mid), content-visibility var(--t-mid) allow-discrete` so `content-visibility` cross-fades through `allow-discrete`. Wrapped in `@supports (interpolate-size: allow-keywords) { ... }` вҖ” older browsers skip the height transition but the chevron still rotates and `<details>` still toggles natively, so the fallback experience is structurally identical, just instant. Pure CSS, **zero JS** for the toggle (`<details>` carries the state). `prefers-reduced-motion: reduce` cancels both the chevron transition and the height transition. **A11y catch:** initial verifier pass had axe `aria-allowed-role` minor Г— 6 вҖ” I'd wrapped the list in `role="list"` + each `<details>` in `role="listitem"` because the visual rhythm reads as a list. axe correctly flagged it: ARIA `listitem` is not allowed on a `<details>` element (which is its own disclosure-widget primitive). Fixed by stripping both attributes вҖ” the `<details>` elements form the semantic structure on their own, and the visual list is a CSS concern. After fix: axe-core 4.10.2 across the entire page (now hero + problem + pillars + steps + grader + pricing + FAQ): **0 violations** at 1440 + 375. **Verified** via `scripts/agent-test/loop47-faq.mjs` (NEW, clone of L46-pricing harness adapted for accordion behaviour) at 1440Г—900 + 375Г—812: 6 `<details>` rendered (every element's `tagName === "DETAILS"`); all 6 expected questions present (verified by exact-match set comparison against the spec appendix #5 list); section title "Usein kysyttyГӨ Puheosta." reads correctly; `summary.click()` flips `el.open === true`, the chevron's CSS transform parses as exactly **90.0В°** (computed via `Math.atan2(b, a) * 180 / Math.PI` on the matrix, see verifier line ~85), the answer panel renders (152 px height desktop, 229 px mobile вҖ” first item is the 7-sentence YTL-endorsement answer); second click flips `el.open` back to `false`. axe at both viewports: **0 violations**. - [2026-04-28 META] [PLAN] Three mid-session updates received from user before Loop 46. ## Landing rebuild вҖ” final (L42 вҶ’ L49)

**Eight loops, one cohesive landing.** `index.html` rewritten from a 1938-line legacy light-mint document into a 756-line dark Linear/Vercel-restraint shell scoped under `<html class="landing">`; ten `<section>` blocks (nav, hero, problem, pillars, steps, grader, pricing, FAQ, CTA, footer) all built off `.landing-section` + token-only CSS in `css/landing.css` (1525 lines) + `css/landing-tokens.css` (156 lines). | Metric | Score | Threshold |
|---|---|---|
| Lighthouse Performance | **97** | вүҘ 95 вң“ |
| Lighthouse Accessibility | **100** | вүҘ 95 вң“ |
| Lighthouse Best Practices | **100** | вүҘ 95 вң“ |
| axe-core violations (375 / 768 / 1024 / 1920) | **0 / 0 / 0 / 0** | 0 вң“ |
| FCP | 0.7 s | < 1.8 s вң“ |
| LCP | 1.1 s | < 2.5 s вң“ |
| TBT | 0 ms | < 200 ms вң“ |
| CLS | 0.001 | < 0.1 вң“ |
| Speed Index | 0.7 s | < 3.4 s вң“ |
| Heading-hierarchy jumps | 0 | 0 вң“ |
| Horizontal scroll @ 375 / 768 / 1024 / 1920 | none | none вң“ |
| `target="_blank"` without `rel=noopener` | 0 | 0 вң“ |

**Final-loop screenshots:** `scripts/agent-test/screenshots/loop49-{375,768,1024,1920}-full.png`. Per-section verification screenshots from L43вҖ“L48 remain alongside.

**21st.dev sourcing trail (L46 вҶ’ L48):** pricing вҶ’ `community/components/efferd/pricing/default`, FAQ вҶ’ `community/components/tailark/faq/faq-accordion-with-title`, final CTA вҶ’ `community/components/dhiluxui/spotlight-cta/default`, footer вҶ’ `community/components/shadcnblockscom/footer-7/default`. All ported React+Tailwind вҶ’ vanilla matching `css/landing.css` patterns. Structure from 21st.dev, copy from Puheo (Finnish, never generic SaaS).

**Deferred / open:**

- **Old `landing.css`** (1332-line light-mint sheet) still on disk and still actively linked by 6 blog pages + 4 legal pages + `sw.js` cache list + 7 unit tests. Deletion punts to **L52вҖ“L55 dark-theme migration** where blog + legal will be ported to the new `.landing`-scoped tokens and their `<link>` swapped to `css/landing.css` + `css/landing-tokens.css`.

Already has `loading="eager" decoding="async" width="1440" height="900"` so LCP lands at 1.1 s on desktop preset; a WebP/AVIF variant would shave a few hundred ms but is not required for the вүҘ 95 gate. `cwebp` / `sharp` are not currently available in the dev env. Punt to a future micro-loop or wire `sharp` as a devDependency if a perf-budget tightening is ever asked for.

  - **Real social-proof numbers** вҖ” the page currently leans on product claims (`2 000+ harjoitustehtГӨvГӨГӨ`, `YTL:n mukainen rubriikki`) rather than user-count or testimonial logos. ## L-PLAN-1 вҖ” onboarding redesign + placement upgrade (2026-04-28)

- **[2026-04-28 L-PLAN-1] UPDATE 1 вҖ” placement-question hardening + adaptive M_hard anchors + timing-confidence helper.** `lib/placementQuestions.js`: every question now carries `plausible_wrong_options: true` after a distractor audit (B5 swapped joke distractor "sГӨГӨ" вҶ’ "kauppa" + "loma"; A1 swapped "kissa" вҶ’ "tie" so all 4 options are physical-place nouns; B/C/M-tier already audited as plausible-only). Added two `M_hard` anchor questions (`MH1` pluskvamperfekti `se habГӯan ido`, `MH2` subjunktiivi imperfekti `si tuviera`) вҖ” only injected by the OB-2 client when the student answers every A/B/C item correctly, signal of potential Kurssi 7 placement. Kept `selectDiagnosticQuestions(...)` returning a flat `Array` (legacy `/api/placement/submit` route still works); added `selectOnboardingQuestions(...)` returning `{ core, mHardCandidates }` for the V2 flow. `lib/placement.js`: new `placementConfidence(answers)` (median `time_ms < 4000` вҶ’ `low`) and `suggestStartingKurssi(level, confidence)` mapping per CURRICULUM_SPEC В§6 (`AвҶ’1, BвҶ’3, CвҶ’5, M+вҶ’7`, вҖ“1 kurssi when confidence is low). All 1 061 vitest tests still pass.
- **[2026-04-28 L-PLAN-1] UPDATE 3 вҖ” `POST /api/placement/onboarding` + `lib/curriculum.js` + tutor-assessment OpenAI call with hardcoded fallback.** New endpoint at `/api/placement/onboarding` (rather than the brief's `/submit` вҖ” `/submit` already exists and serves the legacy diagnostic flow; renaming would break it). Optional-auth wrapper: when a Bearer token is present, persists `self_reported_grade / target_grade / weak_areas / daily_goal_minutes / placement_confidence / placement_kurssi / tutor_assessment / current_grade` to `user_profile` (single upsert); when absent, the endpoint returns the same payload anonymously so the OB-3/OB-4 screens still render. Companion `GET /api/placement/onboarding-questions` exposes the core 8 + 2 M_hard candidates (with answers + Finnish explanations вҖ” placement, not graded, so client-side is fine for inline feedback). New `lib/curriculum.js` carries `KURSSI_META` (key вҶ’ name + level) and the first ~5 lessons of every kurssi (1вҖ“8) sourced verbatim from CURRICULUM_SPEC В§3, plus `generateFirstWeekPlan(kurssiKey, dailyGoalMinutes)` вҖ” deterministic, no AI, with an SR-review tail appended on day 3+ when goal вүҘ30 min вҖ” and `fallbackTutorAssessment(level, kurssi, confidence)` вҖ” template Finnish prose used when the OpenAI call fails so the endpoint never errors. Tutor assessment: `callOpenAI(prompt, 160, { temperature: 0.5 })` returning `{ "tutorAssessment": "вҖҰ" }` (forced JSON object per `puheo-ai-prompt` rule В§2 вҖ” the SDK-wrapper always JSON-parses), prompt prepended with the `puheo-ai-prompt` system preamble verbatim and explicitly forbids abstract level-talk + bullet lists per CURRICULUM_SPEC В§7. Sanity check on AI text (вүҘ30 chars, no leading bullet) before accepting; otherwise template fallback. Curriculum tables not seeded yet вҖ” that's L-PLAN-2; the lesson catalogue here is the bridge.
- **[2026-04-28 L-PLAN-1] UPDATE 2 вҖ” 4 V2 onboarding screens (`#screen-ob1-profile` вҶ’ `#screen-ob2-test` вҶ’ `#screen-ob3-assessment` вҶ’ `#screen-ob4-plan`).** Built side-by-side with the legacy `screen-ob-*` flow (kept untouched per the brief's "do not delete before verifying" rule). New module `js/screens/onboardingV2.js` (state machine, single export `showOnboardingV2()` plus `initOnboardingV2({ loadDashboard })`); new stylesheet `css/components/onboarding-v2.css` token-only (`--bg`, `--surface`, `--ink*`, `--accent*`, `--border*`) with `min-h-100dvh`, max-width 560 px shell, `clamp()`-driven typography, focus rings on every interactive, 44 px touch targets, `prefers-reduced-motion` gating on every transition. **OB-1** uses 4 fields (school grade segmented pill picker вҖ” labelled "viimeisin espanjan arvosanasi koulun kokeessa" per the brief's correction that this is school grade not yo-grade вҖ” target grade with auto-pre-select one notch above school grade, multi-select chips for weak areas with mutually-exclusive "En tiedГӨ vielГӨ", daily-goal pill row 10/20/30/45 min); CTA disabled until both grades chosen. **OB-2** runs the test: progress bar + counter, single question + 4 stacked 56 px options, per-answer timing tracked via `performance.now()` and stored as `time_ms`, instant inline feedback (green/red border + Finnish verdict + `explanation` from `PLACEMENT_QUESTIONS`), auto-advance after 2 s or on tap-anywhere; M_hard anchors injected if no A/B/C error. **OB-3** shows the AI-skeleton then the tutor card (prose, not bullets), 4 horizontal score bars (Sanasto = (A+B)/2, Kielioppi = (B+C)/2, Vaativa taso = M, Kokonaisuus = mean), "Aloitamme [Kurssin N]" line in `--accent`, and the low-confidence note shown only when applicable, framed positively per `self-efficacy-builder-sequence` ("varmistuksen vuoksi"). **OB-4** renders the deterministic `firstWeekPlan` as 5 day-rows (Ma/Ti/Ke/To/Pe) with Lucide-style SVG icons (BookOpen / Wrench / PenLine / Refresh), monospace minute estimates, and a finish CTA that marks legacy `onboarding_completed:true` and routes to the dashboard if logged in or to `/app.html#rekisteroidy` (with the result stashed in `sessionStorage`) otherwise. Hash entry `#/aloitus` triggers V2 from main.js. SW v95вҶ’v96, added `onboarding-v2.css` + `onboardingV2.js` to `STATIC_ASSETS`. All 1 061 vitest tests still pass.

The visual language (token-only dark surface, restrained pill+chip rows, mono day labels, accent-only fills) intentionally matches `references/landing/21stdev/pricing/efferd` from L46. Spec'd in CURRICULUM_SPEC В§8 (sql-block at the bottom).

## L-PLAN-2 вҖ” curriculum structure + Oppimispolku screen (2026-04-29)

- **[2026-04-29 L-PLAN-2] UPDATE 1 вҖ” DB migration `supabase/migrations/20260429_curriculum.sql` + JS mirror `lib/curriculumData.js`.** Migration creates `curriculum_kurssit` (8 rows), `curriculum_lessons` (90 rows total: K1=10, K2=10, K3=11, K4=12, K5=11, K6=12, K7=12, K8=12 вҖ” the brief's "86 total" was an undercount; ground truth is the В§3 line counts), `teaching_pages`, and `user_curriculum_progress` (PK on `user_id, kurssi_key, lesson_index`). Also picks up the **L-PLAN-1 deferred `user_profile` columns** in the same file (`self_reported_grade / target_grade / weak_areas / daily_goal_minutes / placement_confidence / placement_kurssi / tutor_assessment`) so applying this one migration closes the L-PLAN-1 deferred item too. Each kurssi's `grammar_focus` array references **only existing `LEARNING_PATH` keys** (verified via `lib/learningPath.js`): K1 `[present_regular]`, K2 `[present_irregular]`, K3 `[preterite]`, K4 `[imperfect, preterite_vs_imperfect]`, K5 `[future, conditional]`, K6 `[subjunctive_present]`, K7 `[subjunctive_present, pluscuamperfecto]`, K8 `[subjunctive_imperfect]` вҖ” no new keys needed. Each `vocab_theme` references `VALID_VOCAB_TOPICS` from `lib/openai.js` (general vocabulary / travel and transport / environment and nature / work and economy / society and politics / culture and arts). Lessons follow the **worked-example fading** rule: the first lesson of each kurssi has a full worked example in `teaching_snippet` (espanja + suomi + selitys); the last 2 oppituntia before the kertaustesti shrink to a one-hint sentence (prefixed "Vihje:"); each kertaustesti carries the spec's verbatim "Nyt testataan mitГӨ olet oppinut вҖ” [topic]. [X] kysymystГӨ." Backwards-design check: every `focus` field names a measurable sub-goal (e.g. "Preteriti вҖ” sГӨГӨnnГ¶lliset -ar-verbit", not "lesson 2 of kurssi 3"). Interleaving check: vocab + grammar + mixed lessons interleave inside every kurssi per CURRICULUM_SPEC В§3 (no all-vocab-then-all-grammar blocks). Migration NOT auto-applied вҖ” the project doesn't have Supabase CLI configured locally; user applies via Supabase dashboard SQL editor. **JS mirror** `lib/curriculumData.js` exports `CURRICULUM_KURSSIT` + `CURRICULUM_LESSONS` matching the SQL row-for-row, used as fallback by the routes when the tables aren't yet seeded so the UI works pre-migration.
- **[2026-04-29 L-PLAN-2] UPDATE 2 вҖ” `routes/curriculum.js` (4 endpoints) + mounted at `/api/curriculum` in `server.js`.** **GET /api/curriculum** returns `{ kurssit: [{ key, title, description, level, sortOrder, lessonCount, lessonsCompleted, isUnlocked, lastScore, kertausPassed }] }`. Unlock chain: kurssi_1 always unlocked; kurssi_N unlocks when kurssi_{N-1}'s last-lesson kertaustesti score вүҘ 80% (`PASS_THRESHOLD = 0.80`). Anonymous callers see kurssi_1 unlocked + rest locked (matches the brief's empty-state contract). **GET /api/curriculum/:kurssiKey** returns kurssi metadata + per-lesson `{ id, sortOrder, type, focus, exerciseCount, teachingSnippet, completed, score }` joined with `user_curriculum_progress` for authed users. **GET /api/curriculum/:kurssiKey/lesson/:lessonIndex** returns `{ lesson, teachingPage }`. Teaching pages are generated lazily for `grammar` / `mixed` lessons via `callOpenAI(prompt, 400, { temperature: 0.3 })` returning `{ "contentMd": "..." }` (forced JSON object per the lib/openai wrapper), prompt enforces the В§5 structure verbatim (`# title` / 1-paragraph / `## Muodostus` / `## Esimerkki` / `## YO-vinkki рҹ’Ў`), explicitly forbids abstract level-talk + bullets outside tables; cached in `teaching_pages` keyed by `${kurssiKey}_lesson_${sortOrder}`. Hardcoded Finnish fallback when AI fails (>50-char minimum on parsed `contentMd`). **POST /api/curriculum/:kurssiKey/lesson/:lessonIndex/complete** (requireAuth) upserts to `user_curriculum_progress`, computes `kurssiComplete = isKertaustesti && score/total вүҘ 0.80`, generates a `tutorMessage` via OpenAI (success path = "kehu vaikeinta osa-aluetta", remediation path = "nimeГӨ konkreettisesti yksi kielioppirakenne joka tarvitsee lisГӨharjoittelua"; both вүӨ 2 lauseetta, sinГӨ-muoto, ei prosentteja); **hardcoded Finnish fallback** per kurssi name guarantees the endpoint never returns an empty message. Returns `{ kurssiComplete, nextKurssiUnlocked, nextKurssiKey, nextKurssiTitle, tutorMessage, isKertaustesti, passed }`. **`tablesMissing(err)`** helper soft-fails on `42P01` / `PGRST205` / "relation does not exist" so the routes degrade to `lib/curriculumData.js` when the migration hasn't been applied yet вҖ” the screen still loads. Verified end-to-end via `curl /api/curriculum` (200, kurssit list rendered) + `curl /api/curriculum/kurssi_3/lesson/2` (200, OpenAI generated a clean Markdown teaching page with Muodostus table + esimerkki blockquote + YO-vinkki). All 1 061 vitest tests still pass.
- **[2026-04-29 L-PLAN-2] UPDATE 3 вҖ” `#screen-path` rebuilt as 8-kurssi vertical timeline + new `#screen-lesson` + new module `js/screens/curriculum.js` + `css/components/curriculum.css`.** **Screen layout** (max-width 880, mobile collapses to 32 px step circles): vertical `<ol class="curr-list">` with a 1 px linear-gradient connector running through the centre of the step circles (sourced layout pattern: 21st.dev `/s/timeline` + `/s/steps` aesthetic вҖ” restrained dark, single-stroke connector, numbered nodes, no Material-style raised elevation). 8 kurssi cards 80 px tall each: 48 px step circle (filled accent for current/done with check-icon, outline for locked with lock-icon), title + level chip (A/B/C/M/E in `--accent`), Linear-tier progress bar with `aria-valuenow` (`X / Y oppituntia`), status label ("Suoritettu вң“" / "Jatka вҶ’" / "Aloita вҶ’" / "Lukittu"). Locked cards dim to `opacity: 0.45` + `cursor: not-allowed` + `aria-disabled`; current kurssi has `border-left: 3px solid var(--accent)`; done kurssit get muted accent. Tap an unlocked card вҶ’ toggles `is-expanded` (no new screen) and lazy-loads `/api/curriculum/:kurssiKey` to render compact 48 px lesson rows (Lucide-style icons inline as SVG path-d strings: BookOpen=vocab/mixed, Wrench=grammar, BookText=reading, PenLine=writing, CheckSquare=test). Loading state = 8 shimmer skeleton cards (1400 ms gradient sweep, `animation: none` on `prefers-reduced-motion`). Empty state for anonymous = kurssi_1 unlocked + rest locked + RekisterГ¶idy CTA. Error state = retry button. **`#screen-lesson`** (new screen, added to app.html shell): back button вҶ’ `loadCurriculum()`, eyebrow `${typeLabel} В· oppitunti N`, focus title, teaching-page card (max-w 720, dark surface) rendered via in-house **minimal Markdown renderer** (escapes input first, then unwraps headings/blockquotes/4-col tables/inline `**bold**` + `code`); fallback shows the lesson's `teachingSnippet` when no teaching page is available (vocab/test/reading/writing types). Two CTAs: primary `Aloita harjoittelu вҶ’` navigates to the existing exercise screen by lesson type (vocab/mixed вҶ’ `#/sanasto`, grammar вҶ’ `#/puheoppi`, reading вҶ’ `#/luetun`, writing вҶ’ `#/kirjoitus`) and stashes `sessionStorage.currentLesson = { kurssiKey, lessonIndex }` for L-PLAN-3 to pick up; secondary `Merkitse suoritetuksi (vГӨliaikainen)` POSTs to `/complete` with mock score = exerciseCount/exerciseCount and renders the `tutorMessage` in a banner вҖ” temporary scaffold so the loop is closeable manually until L-PLAN-3 wires real exercise scores. **Wired the existing `data-nav="path"` left-nav button** to `loadCurriculum()` in `js/main.js` (legacy `loadPath()` from `learningPath.js` still fires its `nav-path` click binding but bails out gracefully because its target DOM ids `#path-nodes` / `#path-progress-fill` no longer exist after `loadCurriculum()` writes `<div id="curr-root">` into `#screen-path`). Mastery test screens (`#screen-mastery-intro` / `#screen-mastery-result`) left intact вҖ” not on the new flow but reachable via legacy code paths until L-PLAN-3+ replaces them. SW `puheo-v96 вҶ’ puheo-v97`, added `curriculum.css` + `curriculum.js` to `STATIC_ASSETS`. Verified via the live dev server: `/api/curriculum` 200 + first kurssi unlocked + others locked anonymously; `/api/curriculum/kurssi_3/lesson/2` 200 with OpenAI-generated teaching page including Muodostus markdown table.

## L-PLAN-3 вҖ” exercise loop wired to curriculum + dashboard tutor voice (2026-04-29)

- **[2026-04-28 L-PLAN-3] UPDATE 1 вҖ” `lib/lessonContext.js` + curriculum-aware overrides on `/api/generate`, `/api/grammar-drill`, `/api/reading-task`.** New helper `resolveLessonContext({ kurssiKey, lessonIndex })` reads from `curriculum_kurssit` + `curriculum_lessons` in Supabase, falls back to `lib/curriculumData.js` when the migration has not been applied (same `tablesMissing()` short-circuit as routes/curriculum.js). Returns `{ kurssi, lesson, isKertaustesti }`. Companion `curriculumFocusInstruction(ctx)` and `curriculumTestInstruction(ctx)` build the Finnish prompt-augmentation block per CURRICULUM_SPEC В§3 + the brief's retrieval-practice / practice-problem-sequence-designer rules: focus block constrains tehtГӨvГӨt to `lesson.focus`, orders them recognitionвҶ’production, and asks the model to repeat ydinsanoja in the last item so opitut juurtuvat; test block names every `kurssi.grammar_focus[]` topic, demands even coverage, and requires a `topic_key` field on every question (used by UPDATE 2's tutor-message AI to spot which sub-topic produced errors). New `applyLessonContext(reqBody, defaults, kind)` in `routes/exercises.js` resolves the payload `{ lesson: { kurssiKey, lessonIndex } }` (sent by the client when `sessionStorage.currentLesson` is set) and overrides level + topic + count: `level` from `kurssi.level` (AвҶ’B for reading since reading endpoint's lowest tier is B), vocab `topic` from `kurssi.vocab_theme`, `count` from `lesson.exercise_count` (caps the existing 1вҖ“10 clamp at 1вҖ“20 for kertaustesti). Bank lookups + `saveToBankBulk` are bypassed when `lessonCtx` is set so a curriculum-tailored batch never poisons the generic free-practice bank. The lesson focus block is concatenated immediately after `${profileCtx}` so it dominates the prompt without breaking the existing JSON-array output contract. **Frontend wiring**: new `js/lib/lessonContext.js` exposes `getLessonContext()` / `clearLessonContext()`; vocab.js `loadNextBatch` + grammar.js `loadGrammarDrill` + reading.js `loadReadingTask` spread `{ lesson: getLessonContext() }` into the fetch body when context is active. Verified via the live dev server: `curl /api/curriculum` 200, route ordering (literal `/tutor-message` ahead of dynamic `/:kurssiKey`) intact (`curl /api/curriculum/kurssi_3` 200, `curl /api/curriculum/tutor-message` returns `{"message":null}` for anonymous). All 1 061 vitest tests still pass.
- **[2026-04-28 L-PLAN-3] UPDATE 3 вҖ” `GET /api/curriculum/tutor-message` (24h cache via new `user_profile.tutor_greeting` + `tutor_greeting_at` columns) + dashboard tutor card.** Endpoint added to `routes/curriculum.js` and registered BEFORE the dynamic `/:kurssiKey` route so its literal path is not shadowed (the dynamic route would otherwise return 404 "Kurssia ei lГ¶ydy" for `/tutor-message`). `optionalAuth` wrapper: anonymous вҶ’ `{ message: null }` and the dashboard hides the card cleanly. Auth path: reads `user_profile` for `tutor_greeting / tutor_greeting_at / placement_kurssi / weak_areas / exam_date / current_grade / target_grade`, returns the cached message when `< 24h` old (the `intelligent-tutoring-dialogue-designer` skill's "acknowledge specifically + give one concrete next step" rule means the message decays within a day anyway). Cache miss path: pulls the most recent `user_curriculum_progress` row to get last lesson focus + score, derives current kurssi from `placement_kurssi` (or kurssi_1 if unset), computes `daysToExam` against `user_profile.exam_date` (defaults to 28.9.2026 per CURRICULUM_SPEC В§1), pulls `weak_areas[0]` for the heikoin alue line, then calls `callOpenAI(prompt, 80, { temperature: 0.7 })` with the `puheo-ai-prompt` system preamble. Prompt explicitly forbids bullet-lists + numeric pistemГӨГӨrГӨt; gives 3 example-style verbatim quotes from the brief but instructs the model NOT to copy them. Sanity check: вүҘ20 chars, вүӨ300 chars, no leading bullet вҖ” otherwise the time-of-day fallback (`fallbackGreeting()`) fires (4 hardcoded Finnish strings keyed on aamu / pГӨivГӨ / ilta / yo Г— lastFocus / weakArea / kurssiTitle / daysToExam priority). On AI success the message is upserted to `user_profile.tutor_greeting` + `tutor_greeting_at`; the upsert is `tablesMissing`-soft so pre-migration users still get a fresh response on every load. Migration `supabase/migrations/20260429_curriculum.sql` extended with `ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS tutor_greeting text` + `tutor_greeting_at timestamptz` so applying that one file still closes the L-PLAN-1, L-PLAN-2, and L-PLAN-3 DB work. **Frontend**: new `<section class="dash-tutor">` + skeleton card inserted into `app.html` directly under the existing `header.dash-greeting`; dashboard.js `loadTutorMessage()` (kicked off in parallel with `renderDashboard`) reads `sessionStorage.dashTutorMsg` (per-tab cache so the card does not blink on every render), falls back to a 2-line shimmer skeleton on cache miss, and hides itself entirely on anonymous / null / fetch error. CSS in `css/components/dashboard.css` (max-width 640, accent left-border 3 px, line-height 1.6, `prefers-reduced-motion` gates the shimmer). Verified anonymous response above; auth-path manual smoke pending Supabase migration application.
- **[2026-04-28 L-PLAN-3] UPDATE 2 вҖ” post-session lesson results card + extended `/complete` endpoint.** **Server**: `POST /api/curriculum/:kurssiKey/lesson/:lessonIndex/complete` now accepts `{ scoreCorrect, scoreTotal, wrongAnswers[], lessonType }` in the body. `wrongAnswers` is sanitised (вүӨ20 entries, every string field clamped to 200 chars) and folded into a single `callOpenAI(prompt, 200, { temp 0.5 })` call that returns BOTH `tutorMessage` (2вҖ“3 lauseetta, lГӨmmin + spesifi, formative-assessment-loop-designer rule: identifies the gap + names the very next step; on kertaustesti the path branches between menestys / kertaa) AND `metacognitivePrompt` (TARKASTI 1 lause neutraali reflektiohuomio per metacognitive-prompt-library skill: not a question, but a pattern observation like "Huomasit varmasti, ettГӨ preteriti -ir verbeissГӨ on eri pГӨГӨte kuin -ar verbeissГӨ"). Both fields fall back to score-band-keyed Finnish templates when the AI returns blank or fails вҖ” endpoint never errors. New `checkFastTrack(userId, kurssiKey)` helper queries the last 3 progress rows for the kurssi and returns true only when ALL three are вүҘ85% (flow-state-condition-designer rule: 3 perГӨttГӨistГӨ >85% вҶ’ tarjoa hyppy, mutta valinta jГӨtetГӨГӨn oppilaalle). Response now also includes `metacognitivePrompt` + `fastTrack` fields; existing fields `kurssiComplete / nextKurssiUnlocked / nextKurssiKey / nextKurssiTitle / tutorMessage / isKertaustesti / passed` unchanged. **Frontend**: new module `js/screens/lessonResults.js` with single export `showLessonResults({ kurssiKey, lessonIndex, lessonFocus, lessonType, scoreCorrect, scoreTotal, wrongAnswers })`. Sourced layout pattern: 21st.dev `/s/results` + `/s/score-card` register вҖ” restrained single-column dark card with mono score, single-stroke accuracy bar (animated width 600 ms cubic-bezier, gated by `prefers-reduced-motion`), three text blocks (score вҶ’ metacognitive-italic вҶ’ tutor-prose) + actions stack. Fast-track callout renders inline with `[KyllГӨ]` / `[Ei, jatkan tГӨstГӨ]` only when `resp.fastTrack === true`. Primary CTA always "Jatka oppimispolkua вҶ’" (clears `sessionStorage.currentLesson` + invalidates the dashboard tutor cache + calls `loadCurriculum()`); secondary CTA "Aloita [next kurssi title] вҶ’" only when kurssiComplete && nextKurssiKey. Score colour: `--accent` (вүҘ80%), `--warn` (60вҖ“79%), `--err` (<60%). `curriculum.js` openLesson now stashes `lessonFocus` + `lessonType` into `sessionStorage.currentLesson` after the lesson fetch resolves so the results card has the data without a second fetch. Each of vocab.js / grammar.js / reading.js short-circuits its legacy results screen at the top of `showVocabResults` / `showGrammarResults` / `showReadingResults`: when `getLessonContext()` returns context, it builds `wrongAnswers[]` from the existing per-mode session state (vocab `state.sessionItems`, grammar `state.grammarUserAnswers` joined with `state.grammarExercises` to extract correct option text + rule, reading sends `[]` since the mode tracks only an aggregate `state.readingScore`), still calls `_deps.saveProgress(...)` so the regular dashboard analytics fire, then dynamic-imports `lessonResults.js` and hands off. **Removed the temporary `Merkitse suoritetuksi (vГӨliaikainen)` button** from `js/screens/curriculum.js` `renderLessonPage` along with the now-dead `markComplete()` helper and `#curr-tutor-banner` markup вҖ” the real flow above replaces it. New `#screen-lesson-results` div added to `app.html` shell. CSS appended to `css/components/curriculum.css` (~140 lines, token-only, no new dependencies). SW `puheo-v97 вҶ’ puheo-v98`, added `lessonResults.js` + `lessonContext.js` to STATIC_ASSETS. All 1 061 vitest tests still pass.

**Deferred from L-PLAN-3 (not blocking L-PLAN-4):**
- **Apply the migration to Supabase.** Migration file extended in this loop with two new columns (`user_profile.tutor_greeting` + `tutor_greeting_at`); still no Supabase CLI configured locally вҖ” user runs `supabase/migrations/20260429_curriculum.sql` once via the dashboard SQL editor. Until then the tutor-message endpoint serves a fresh AI response on every call (no cache hit), `user_curriculum_progress` writes silently no-op (so fast-track + curriculum unlock chain only behaves once the migration is applied), and the JS-mirror fallback keeps the UI rendering. This is the same deferred item as L-PLAN-2's; the columns added in this loop fold into it.
- **axe-core sweep at 1440 + 375 on `#screen-lesson-results` + dashboard with the new tutor card.** No script written this loop. Markup follows the same a11y patterns L-PLAN-2's curriculum.js verified clean (real `<button>` elements, `role="progressbar"` with valuenow/min/max on the accuracy bar, `aria-live="polite"` on the tutor card, `aria-busy="true"` on skeleton lines, contrast on `--ink-soft` against `--surface` measured вүҘ 4.7:1 in the existing token system). Worth one verification loop before the next major UI iteration.
- **21st.dev Playwright sourcing pass for `/s/results` + `/s/score-card`** вҖ” built directly from spec to keep momentum on the curriculum loop. The card's visual register intentionally matches L46's `efferd/pricing` (single-column dark surface, accent-toned scores, no celebration) so a future polish loop can capture references and cross-check without a rebuild.
- **Real per-question student/correct text in reading mode.** Reading currently only tracks an aggregate `state.readingScore`; the wrongAnswers payload is empty for reading sessions, so the AI tutorMessage works from score + lesson focus alone for that mode. Extending `js/screens/reading.js` `handleAnswer` to record per-question chosen/correct strings would let the AI cite exact reading-comprehension errors. Not blocking вҖ” the AI fallback templates still fire when wrongAnswers is empty.
- **Reading lessons in the Kurssi 1вҖ“2 range.** Kurssi 1/2 are A-level; the reading-task endpoint's lowest tier is B. `applyLessonContext` maps A вҶ’ B so the request still succeeds, but those kurssit have no reading lessons in the curriculum (verified `curriculumData.js`) вҖ” this is a defensive code path that won't fire in practice.

## L-PLAN-4 вҖ” UI fixes + DB migration ACTION REQUIRED + V2 default + streak bridge + fast-leveling UI (2026-04-29)

- **[2026-04-29 L-PLAN-4] UPDATE 1 вҖ” Supabase migration verified, ACTION REQUIRED for the user.** Re-read `supabase/migrations/20260429_curriculum.sql` end-to-end: every required table is present (`curriculum_kurssit`, `curriculum_lessons`, `teaching_pages`, `user_curriculum_progress` + `idx_user_curriculum_progress_user`) and the `ALTER TABLE user_profile` block carries all 9 columns the endpoints touch (`self_reported_grade`, `target_grade`, `weak_areas`, `daily_goal_minutes`, `placement_confidence`, `placement_kurssi`, `tutor_assessment`, `tutor_greeting`, `tutor_greeting_at`; `current_grade` exists on the table from earlier work). Idempotent вҖ” `CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS` + `ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS`, safe to run as many times as needed. **=== ACTION REQUIRED вҖ” SUPABASE MIGRATION ===** the user runs this once via the Supabase SQL editor (`https://supabase.com/dashboard/project/_/sql`); after that the "Ladataan oppituntojaвҖҰ" dead-state on the Oppimispolku screen disappears, `user_curriculum_progress` writes start landing, and the dashboard tutor-message starts hitting its 24h cache instead of regenerating each load. Until then every endpoint degrades gracefully via `tablesMissing()` + the `lib/curriculumData.js` JS mirror. Marked deferred items from L-PLAN-1, L-PLAN-2, L-PLAN-3 closed-pending-user.
- **[2026-04-29 L-PLAN-4] UPDATE 2 вҖ” global scroll-to-top fix + scroll-padding for sticky offsets.** Root cause: `show()` (`js/ui/nav.js`) only swapped the `.active` class without resetting `window.scrollY`, so navigating from a long screen (Puheoppi after expanding all topics) to a shorter one (`#screen-grammar` exercise screen) preserved the previous scroll offset and the new H1 sat above the visible viewport вҖ” exactly the "menee piiloon tonne ylГ¶s" pattern the user reported "now in many places". Fix: `show()` calls `window.scrollTo({ top: 0, left: 0, behavior: "auto" })` after every screen swap; `style.css` adds `--header-height: 72px` token + `html { scroll-padding-top: var(--header-height); }` + `.screen h1, .screen h2, .screen [data-scroll-anchor] { scroll-margin-top: var(--header-height); }` so any scrollIntoView / hash anchor lands below the fixed `app-countdown` bar (34 px) plus a 38 px visual buffer. Pure JS+CSS, low risk. Skill applied: `cognitive-load-analyser` вҖ” moving the "where am I" reset to the platform layer means individual screens stop having to remember to reset scroll on entry.
- **[2026-04-29 L-PLAN-4] UPDATE 3 вҖ” Puheoppi heading clip + visual breathing room.** Added `scroll-margin-top: var(--header-height)` on `.mode-page .display` + `.mode-page .eyebrow` and `margin-top: 8px` on the leading eyebrow so the eyebrow + display heading block has air at the top of the screen. Combined with UPDATE 2's window-scroll reset, the Puheoppi H1 now lands cleanly under the fixed top bar (вүҘ 56 px main gutter + 34 px countdown shift = 90 px buffer) instead of being cut off mid-glyph. No restructure of the Puheoppi mode-page itself вҖ” the eyebrow + h1 + sub paragraph + briefing card layout already follows `puheo-screen-template`; the bug was platform-wide, not Puheoppi-specific.
- **[2026-04-29 L-PLAN-4] UPDATE 4 вҖ” right rail removed, floating profile button + dropdown replace it (sourced: shadcn/ui DropdownMenu via Radix primitive, ported to vanilla CSS + Puheo token system).** Largest UI change of the loop. **app.html**: stripped `.app-rail` content (`rail-panel--daily` with the daily goal + Sana pГӨivГӨssГӨ, `rail-pro-badge`, `rail-footer`); replaced with a single `aside.profile-menu-wrap` carrying the avatar trigger + dropdown menu. **css/components/app-shell.css**: grid is now permanently 2-column (sidebar + main); `.app-rail` falls back to `display: none !important` defensively so cached older app.html still renders the new layout; `.app-main` reserves 88 px right padding so the floating button never overlaps headings. **css/components/profile-menu.css** (NEW): 40 px gradient avatar, 260 px dropdown anchored top-right with `top: calc(100% + 8px); right: 0;`, body:has-supported countdown-aware top offset, restrained dark register with `color-mix(--accent, --surface)` accents, `prefers-reduced-motion` gates the 120 ms fade, focus ring meets 3:1 against the dark surface. **js/features/profileMenu.js** (NEW): single `initProfileMenu({ startCheckout, updateSidebarState })` called once from `js/main.js`; click toggles `aria-expanded` + `is-open`, ArrowDown/Up cycle items, Home/End jump, Escape closes + returns focus to the trigger, click-outside closes. Items: Top section (avatar + name + email), Oma sivu (forwards to existing sidebar nav), Asetukset, PГӨivitГӨ Pro (free users only вҖ” hidden when `pro === true`), Kirjaudu ulos (clears auth + bounces to `screen-auth`). **dashboard.js renderRail** rewritten to forward the Pro flag to `window._profileMenuRef.syncProfileMenu({ pro })` instead of mutating the now-absent rail DOM. **app.html `.dash-greeting`** gets a streak chip (`.dash-greeting__streak`) hidden until streak вүҘ 1 вҖ” surfaces what used to live in the rail per the spec's KRIITTINEN check. CSS for the chip lives in `css/components/dashboard.css`. SW bump v98 вҶ’ v99 with `profile-menu.css` + `profileMenu.js` added to STATIC_ASSETS. - **[2026-04-29 L-PLAN-4] UPDATE 5 вҖ” streak bridge from curriculum/complete.** `routes/curriculum.js` `POST /complete` now writes a row to `exercise_logs` (NOT `user_sessions` вҖ” verified the actual table name in `routes/progress.js` calculateStreak path) immediately after the `user_curriculum_progress` upsert. Mode is mapped from `lesson.type` to the existing `VALID_MODES` set (`vocab|grammar|reading|writing|exam`; `mixed вҶ’ grammar`, `test вҶ’ exam`) so the row is shaped identically to free-practice writes. Defensive try/catch вҖ” never blocks the endpoint over the bridge. After this change, the dashboard streak counter ticks up after every curriculum-lesson finish, matching free-practice behaviour. - **[2026-04-29 L-PLAN-5] UPDATE 1 вҖ” vocab/reading/writing teaching pages now lazy-generate.** `routes/curriculum.js` `getOrGenerateTeachingPage()` previously short-circuited for any lesson type other than `grammar`/`mixed`; that's why "Numerot ja ikГӨ" (vocab, lesson 6) had no opetussivu when the user opened it. Refactored to a per-type prompt (`buildTeachingPrompt`) + per-type fallback (`buildTeachingFallback`) covering `vocab` (table of 8вҖ“12 ydinsanaa + Muista nГӨmГӨ + YO-vinkki), `reading` (lukustrategia bullets + YO-vinkki вҖ” ei full text, koska itse luettu teksti tulee `/api/reading-task`-endpointilta), `writing` (rakennevinkki bullet-list + MistГӨ saat pisteitГӨ -taulukko + esimerkkilause + YO-vinkki). max_tokens scaled per type (vocab 600, writing 450, others 400) since the vocab table is the longest payload. All cached in `teaching_pages` with the same `${kurssiKey}_lesson_${sortOrder}` key вҖ” re-opening the lesson hits the cache, not OpenAI. Skills applied: `education/explicit-instruction-sequence-builder` (each opetussivu opens with a 1-paragraph "miksi" frame, then naming-of-parts table, then YO-vinkki = "you do" preview), `education/competency-unpacker` (vocab teaching page splits the topic into 8вҖ“12 nimettyГӨ alaosaa rather than one blob), `education/cognitive-load-analyser` (every opetussivu stays at вүӨ4 distinct rakenneosat вҖ” 1 paragraph + 1 table + 1 sudenkuopat-block + 1 YO-vinkki). `puheo-ai-prompt`: every prompt is JSON-forced via `callOpenAI(prompt, max, { temp 0.3 })` per the skill's house style.
- **[2026-04-29 L-PLAN-5] UPDATE 2 вҖ” `#screen-lesson` rebuild: real opetussivu, no stub-only snippet.** `js/screens/curriculum.js` `renderLessonPage()` now builds: (a) eyebrow `Kurssi N В· Oppitunti M` (uppercased per spec, `text-transform: uppercase` in CSS), (b) display H1 sized `clamp(28px, 4.6vw, 40px)` carrying the lesson focus, (c) Markdown card via the existing in-house renderer вҖ” extended with h3 + ul + `*italic*` support so the new vocab/reading/writing prompts render correctly, (d) primary CTA whose label includes both exercise count and estimated duration: `Aloita harjoittelu (10 tehtГӨvГӨГӨ, ~15 min) вҶ’`.
