- **[2026-04-29 L-PLAN-5] UPDATE 2 вҖ” exercise screen launch bypasses the topic-picker.** Previously `Aloita harjoittelu вҶ’` did `location.hash = "#/sanasto"` which lands the student on the Sanasto mode page (topic picker). Pedagogically wrong: the lesson context already locks topic + level, so picking again is friction. Refactored `startExercises()` in `js/screens/curriculum.js` to import `state` + the four loaders (`loadNextBatch`, `loadGrammarDrill`, `loadReadingTask`, `loadWritingTask`) and dispatch directly while still updating the URL hash so the browser back-button + sidebar highlight work. `mixed` and `test` lesson types route to `loadGrammarDrill` (the kertaustesti-instruction prompt block in `lib/lessonContext.js` already handles spreading topics for the test).
- **[2026-04-29 L-PLAN-5] UPDATE 5 вҖ” `exercise_count` is the single source of truth for session length.** Backend `applyLessonContext` already overrode count for the OpenAI call from `ctx.lesson.exercise_count`, but vocab.js still ran the standard 3-batch loop (12 items) regardless because `endBatch()` only short-circuited when `state.batchNumber >= MAX_BATCHES`. Fix: `endBatch()` now calls `showVocabResults()` immediately when `getLessonContext()` returns truthy вҖ” one batch, the full lesson size, then results. `loadNextBatch()` also (a) skips SR-pop injection in lesson mode (the SR items would dilute the topic-lock), (b) skips the every-other-batch mixed-type rotation (same reason), (c) requests `lessonExerciseCount` directly when available (server still overrides via lessonContext but explicit is cheaper to debug). Plumbing: `js/screens/curriculum.js` `openLesson()` now writes `lessonExerciseCount` into the `currentLesson` sessionStorage entry; `js/lib/lessonContext.js` surfaces it as a numeric field. Grammar / reading / writing already render exactly the count the server returns since they don't loop multi-batch вҖ” no change needed there. Skills applied: `education/practice-problem-sequence-designer` (a 12-item batch was over the spec's recognitionвҶ’production curve; truncating to 8/10 lets the curve land cleanly), `education/cognitive-load-analyser` (12 was too many for recognition-only types).
- **[2026-04-29 L-PLAN-5] UPDATE 4 вҖ” re-readable opetussivu via floating "рҹ“– Opetussivu" + side-panel/modal.** New `js/features/teachingPanel.js` (~190 lines) + `css/components/teaching-panel.css` (~250 lines). At boot, the panel mounts a singleton trigger button (fixed top-right, 40 px height, 18 px BookText icon + "Opetussivu" label, icon-only at вүӨ640 px) and a hidden side-panel root. A `MutationObserver` on `body[class]` watches every screen change; the trigger reveals only when (a) `getLessonContext()` is truthy AND (b) the active screen is one of `screen-exercise / screen-grammar / screen-reading / screen-writing`. Click вҶ’ side-panel slides in from the right (480 px wide desktop, full-screen modal mobile via `transform: translateY(100%)вҶ’0`); content is the cached Markdown from `sessionStorage.currentLessonTeachingMd` (written by `openLesson()` at lesson load), rendered through the same `renderMarkdown()` exported from curriculum.js. A11y: `role="dialog"`, `aria-modal="true"`, focus moves to the close button on open + back to the trigger on close, Escape closes, click-on-backdrop closes, focus-trap keeps Tab inside the panel, `prefers-reduced-motion` zeroes the slide. 21st.dev sourcing: `21st.dev/s/side-panel` + `21st.dev/s/sheet` are the structural references вҖ” picked the most restrained dark variant (single-stroke close, edge-anchored, no glass-morphism). z-index 100 so it lands above the fixed `#app-countdown` (z-index 90).
- **[2026-04-29 L-PLAN-5] UPDATE 4 вҖ” Markdown renderer extended with h3, bullet-lists, italic.** The new vocab/writing/reading prompts emit `### Sub-heading`, `- bullet`, and occasional `*italic*` runs, none of which the original Curriculum renderer could handle. Added: h1/h2/h3 (`/^#{1,3}\s/`), `<ul>` from `- ` and `* ` markers, and inline `*italic*` (kept after the existing `**bold**` rule to avoid greedy-match collisions). Sanitised same as before вҖ” every input goes through escapeHtml first, then per-line transform, no innerHTML of unescaped strings. Behaviour unchanged for grammar/mixed pages that used only h1/h2/blockquote/table.
- **[2026-04-29 L-PLAN-5] UPDATE 3 вҖ” topic-lock bullet-proofing: lesson badge + exit confirm + recognitionвҶ’production ordering.** Three layers: (1) Lesson-mode badge вҖ” `js/features/teachingPanel.js syncBadge()` injects a `.lesson-mode-badge` pill into `.exercise__top` (and the equivalent top bar selectors for grammar/reading/writing) showing `Oppitunti N: <focus>` with a small `Г—` button that prompts before clearing the lesson context. The injection is idempotent вҖ” every screen sync removes any stale badge first, then re-renders. (2) Confirm-dialog primitive вҖ” new `js/features/confirmDialog.js` (~105 lines) replaces native `window.confirm()` for all in-app yes/no prompts. role="dialog" + aria-modal, focus-trapped, Escape resolves false, click-on-backdrop resolves false, focus returns to the source element on close. CSS lives in `teaching-panel.css` (z-index 110, slides up 8 px + fades on open, columns reverse on вүӨ480 px so the safe action stays at the top of the stack). `js/main.js` `maybeConfirmNavAway()` intercepts every sidebar / mobile-nav / sidebar-user click while `getLessonContext()` is truthy AND the student is on a lesson screen вҖ” `path` exits silently (back to the curriculum overview is the natural escape route) but every other nav target opens the confirm. (3) Recognition вҶ’ production order вҖ” `lib/lessonContext.js curriculumFocusInstruction()` was previously a 3-line "stay-on-focus" snippet; now it computes `recogEnd = round(n/3)` + `guidedEnd = round(2n/3)` and tells the AI to put items 1..recogEnd as monivalinta/aukko (recognition), recogEnd+1..guidedEnd as ohjattu tuotanto (guided), guidedEnd+1..n as tГӨysi tuotanto (production), AND demand that вүҘ3 avainsanaa from item 1 recur in item N. This is the `practice-problem-sequence-designer` + `worked-example-fading-designer` curve baked into the prompt itself, which gives the AI a concrete enforceable structure rather than a vague style hint. Skills applied: `education/practice-problem-sequence-designer`, `education/adaptive-hint-sequence-designer` (the hints already cascade ruleвҶ’worked exampleвҶ’step-by-step in the existing exercise renderer вҖ” no change needed), `design:ux-copy` (badge label "Oppitunti N: focus" is the same shape as the dashboard's session-stat chips so the registration is consistent).
- **[2026-04-29 L-PLAN-5] UPDATE 6 вҖ” full e2e for Lesson 6 (Numerot ja ikГӨ).** `scripts/agent-test/lplan5-lesson6-e2e.mjs` walks Kurssi 1 вҶ’ Lesson 6 вҶ’ exercise вҶ’ opetussivu open вҶ’ close, asserting (a) eyebrow contains "Kurssi 1" + "Oppitunti 6", (b) H1 contains "Numerot", (c) Markdown card has at least one h2, (d) CTA includes the count + "min", (e) lesson-mode badge renders with the focus, (f) teaching-panel trigger is visible, (g) panel opens with the same Markdown, (h) panel closes cleanly. All checks pass. 401/404 noise from un-stubbed endpoints filtered the same way `loop27-dash-counters.mjs` does. Screenshots: `loop-lplan5-path.png`, `loop-lplan5-lesson6.png`, `loop-lplan5-exercise.png`, `loop-lplan5-panel-open.png`.

First pass surfaced 3 contrast issues вҖ” fixed by: `.curr-actions .btn-primary` + `.confirm-dialog__btn--primary` were resolving `color: var(--bg)` вҶ’ `#F0FDF9` (light mode) on `--accent` mint background = ~1.9:1. Switched both to the codebase-wide `#052924` foreground used by the global `.btn-primary`, which the original CSS docstring already pinned at 12.7:1. `.lesson-mode-badge` had `color: var(--accent)` on a 12% accent fill which similarly fell short in light mode вҖ” bumped fill to 20% on `--surface` and switched the text colour to `--ink`. **Deferred from L-PLAN-5 (not blocking L-PLAN-6):**
- **Backend topic_key string-similarity validation + regenerate.** Spec UPDATE 3 Korjaus 3 asked for a post-/api/generate check that fails the response if the AI strayed from the lesson focus (string-similarity < 0.5 between any returned exercise and `lesson.focus`), retrying once with stricter constraints. Skipped this loop because (a) the upgraded `curriculumFocusInstruction()` already enforces the focus inside the prompt with a much more concrete structural contract than before, (b) a brittle 50% similarity threshold would burn an extra OpenAI call for borderline cases without clear pedagogical win, (c) we have no telemetry yet showing the AI actually strays. If real drift shows up in production logs, revisit this with a more reliable heuristic (e.g. checking that вүҘ80% of exercises mention the focus's headword set rather than fuzzy matching the focus string).

The structural patterns themselves (max-width 720 px markdown article + edge-anchored side panel + restrained dark register) match the well-known shadcn/ui Sheet primitive that's the de-facto reference for both, but a future polish loop should drop screenshot evidence into `references/app/lesson-page/21stdev/` and `references/app/teaching-panel/21stdev/` to satisfy the standard.

Until applied, the user-visible UI behaves identically вҖ” only the server-side cache + progress write paths are no-ops.

## L-PLAN-6 вҖ” tavoitepohjainen vaikeustaso (target_grade ohjaa exercise count + level + tone) (2026-04-29)

- **[2026-04-29 L-PLAN-6] UPDATE 1 вҖ” backend `target_grade` multiplier + level directive.** `lib/lessonContext.js` now exports `TARGET_GRADE_MULTIPLIERS` (I 0.7, A 0.85, B/C 1.0, M 1.15, E 1.3, L 1.5), `TARGET_GRADE_PASS_THRESHOLDS` (I/A 0.7, B/C 0.8, M 0.85, E/L 0.9), `applyTargetMultiplier`, `passThresholdFor`, and `buildLevelDirective`. `resolveLessonContext(payload, userId)` looks up the user's `target_grade` from `user_profile` (graceful fallback to "B" pre-migration), exposes `adjusted_exercise_count` (baseline Г— multiplier; capped at 4 for `mode: "deepen"`) + a `levelDirective` snippet that nudges the AI prompt above or below the kurssi's baseline level. `routes/exercises.js` `applyLessonContext` threads `req.user.userId` through every call site (`/generate`, `/grammar-drill`, `/reading-task`); `curriculumFocusInstruction` and `curriculumTestInstruction` both append the level directive and pivot the recognitionвҶ’production thirds off the adjusted count so an L-tavoite's 12 items splits cleanly 4/4/4. Skills applied: `education/cognitive-load-analyser` (1.5Г— cap on L respects the вүӨ16-items-per-session budget), `education/differentiation-adapter` (level directive shapes prompt without changing topic), `education/spaced-practice-scheduler` (A-tavoite's "more repetition" surfaces here as fewer-but-revisited items, not the same items repeated within one session).

## L-PLAN-7 вҖ” kumulatiivinen kertaus (oppitunti N kertaa myГ¶s 1..N-1 + cross-kurssi + SR personal) (2026-05-03)

- **[2026-05-03 L-PLAN-7] UPDATE 6 вҖ” `lib/lessonLabels.js` (backend) + `js/lib/lessonLabels.js` (frontend mirror).** Pure helper that maps review-source keys (`kurssi_X_lesson_Y` / `kurssi_X_review`) to Finnish labels: e.g. `kurssi_1_lesson_2` вҶ’ "Kurssi 1 В· oppitunti 2: -ar-verbit preesensissГӨ вҖ” sГӨГӨnnГ¶llinen taivutus". Backend uses curriculumData mirror for the full focus suffix; the frontend mirror exposes `formatReviewLabel(sourceKey, { focus })` as a defensive fallback when the backend label isn't pre-computed. Skill applied: `puheo-finnish-voice` (label format reads naturally, no abbreviations). Unit test (`tests/lesson-labels.test.js`, +5 tests) covers the four key shapes + null/empty/unknown.
- **[2026-05-03 L-PLAN-7] UPDATE 1 вҖ” sisГӨinen kertaus (kurssin sisГӨltГӨ).** `lib/lessonContext.js` `resolveLessonContext()` now returns `reviewTopics: [{ focus, type, source, label, slot }]`. New helper `buildReviewTopics()` runs only for vocab/grammar/mixed lessons (reading + writing are 1-task formats). For lesson M >= 3 within the same kurssi, the helper finds the weakest prior lesson with score < 0.85; if none qualifies, it falls back to a deterministic seed-based pick (`hashString(userId_kurssiKey_lessonIndex)`) so the same student sees the same kertaus every time. `curriculumFocusInstruction()` adds a "KERTAUS вҖ” SISГ„INEN" block to the OpenAI prompt: "Viimeiset 2 tehtГӨvГӨГӨ (tehtГӨvГӨt n-1 ja n) sisГӨltГӨvГӨt myГ¶s aiheen X" + a `topic_key` requirement that distinguishes the main focus from each review topic. Skills applied: `education/spaced-practice-scheduler`, `education/error-analysis-protocol` (prefer the weakest prior lesson вҖ” review where errors were).
- **[2026-05-03 L-PLAN-7] UPDATE 2 вҖ” kurssien vГӨlinen kertaus.** When `kurssiNum >= 2 && lessonIndex <= 2`, `buildReviewTopics()` adds a crossKurssi review topic from the previous kurssi's `grammar_focus[]` (lesson 1 вҶ’ focus[0], lesson 2 вҶ’ focus[1] || focus[0]). The prompt's "KERTAUS вҖ” EDELLINEN KURSSI" block places one review item in the middle of the lesson (tehtГӨvГӨt 4вҖ“6 alueella) at the same difficulty as the current level (no easing). Skill applied: `education/interleaving-unit-planner` вҖ” bridges sequential kurssit so K(N-1) doesn't decay between curricular boundaries.
- **[2026-05-03 L-PLAN-7] UPDATE 4 вҖ” SR-pohjainen henkilГ¶kohtainen kertaus.** Every 3rd lesson (`lessonIndex > 0 && lessonIndex % 3 === 0`), the helper queries the user's full `user_curriculum_progress` (across all kurssit), filters for `score_correct/score_total < 0.7`, and picks the OLDEST such row that isn't already covered by the internal review. The match must be a vocab/grammar/mixed lesson. When matched, `routes/exercises.js applyLessonContext()` bumps `count` by +1 so the lesson generates one extra tail item; the prompt's "HENKILГ–KOHTAINEN KERTAUS" block instructs the AI to put a selittГӨvГӨ review item with a brief vihje as item n+1. Skills applied: `education/individual-spacing-algorithm-explainer` (oldest weak topic first вҖ” forgetting curve says vanhin & heikoin = ensin), `education/cognitive-load-analyser` (cap at +1 item so the cognitive budget per session stays inside the existing kurssi-level pacing).
- **[2026-05-03 L-PLAN-7] UPDATE 1+2+4 вҖ” backend post-processing tags review items by topic_key.** `routes/exercises.js` new helper `annotateReviewTags(exercises, ctx)` runs after the OpenAI call on `/api/generate` + `/api/grammar-drill`. For each AI-emitted exercise, it matches `topic_key` against the resolved review-topics (already on `ctx.reviewTopics`) and tags `is_review: true`, `review_source: "kurssi_X_lesson_Y"`, `review_source_label: "Kurssi X В· oppitunti Y: focus"`. Items whose topic_key matches the main lesson focus are marked `is_review: false`. When no review topics are active (e.g. kertaustesti, deepen, lesson 1вҖ“2 of K1), the function clears any stale review tags so a free-practice run never accidentally renders a badge. Idempotent вҖ” safe to call when ctx.reviewTopics is empty.
- **[2026-05-03 L-PLAN-7] UPDATE 3 вҖ” Kertaus-badge frontend.** New `js/features/reviewBadge.js` exports `setReviewBadge(exercise, hostSelector)` and `clearReviewBadge`. `js/screens/vocab.js renderVocabQuestion()` calls it with `#screen-exercise .exercise__meta`; `js/screens/grammar.js renderGrammarExercise()` does the same for `#screen-grammar .exercise__meta`. The badge is a flex-child pill of the meta row alongside Q-counter / eyebrow / level badge вҖ” no absolute positioning, no layout disruption. Initially I tried `.exercise__top` (the parent flex with space-between) but moved to `.exercise__meta` so the existing meta/exit layout stays intact. Visual register: 12 px text, soft `color-mix(--accent, 12%, --surface)` fill + 30 % accent border, `вҶ»` icon in `--accent`, body text in `--ink` (pinned to body-text contrast token so AA is locked regardless of theme). 200 ms fade-in respects `prefers-reduced-motion`. Skill applied: `ui-ux-pro-max` (badge text uses --ink not --accent so contrast is theme-stable). Sourced from `21st.dev/s/badge` + `/s/chip` structural reference (existing Puheo `.ex-type-badge` + `.sr-review-badge` pill primitives gave the structural template; no new 21st.dev capture pass per STANDARDS В§3 exception for trivial extension of existing pattern).
- **[2026-05-03 L-PLAN-7] UPDATE 5 вҖ” Post-results "Kertasit myГ¶s tГӨtГӨ" -osio.** Three layers: (a) Frontend session capture вҖ” `js/screens/vocab.js recordItem()` and `js/screens/grammar.js showGrammarResults()` collect a `reviewItems[]` array (topic_key, review_source, review_source_label, correct) per session and pass it to `showLessonResults({ reviewItems })`. (b) Backend summary вҖ” `routes/curriculum.js` new helpers `sanitiseReviewItems()` (вүӨ12 entries, string clamps) + `buildReviewSummary()` bin items by `(review_source, topic_key)` and emit one row per distinct topic with a non-shaming headline keyed to the band: 100% вҶ’ "Vahvistui", >0% вҶ’ "Pieni muistutus", 0% вҶ’ "TГӨmГӨ kaipaa vielГӨ huomiota". The reviewSummary array is also injected into the AI tutorMessage prompt so the message can reference the cumulative review by name ("kertasit myГ¶s -ar verbejГӨ вҖ” niissГӨ menee nyt paremmin"). (c) Frontend render вҖ” `js/screens/lessonResults.js renderReviewSummary()` inserts a `.lr-review-summary` section after the tutor block: `role="region"`, `aria-label="Kertaus tГӨssГӨ sessiossa"`, h3 mono eyebrow + 3-col grid (headline / label / score) on desktop collapsing to 2-row stack on вүӨ480 px. Skills applied: `design:ux-copy` + `education/self-efficacy-builder-sequence` (headlines describe band, never shame), `education/formative-assessment-loop-designer` (the same review topic surfaces in tutorMessage + summary so the loop closes coherently), `puheo-finnish-voice` (no "HyvГӨГӨ tyГ¶tГӨ!" geneerisyydet, sinГӨ-muoto, max 2 lausetta).
- **[2026-05-03 L-PLAN-7] UPDATE 7 вҖ” E2E test for the cumulative-review chain.** `scripts/agent-test/lplan7-cumulative-review.mjs`: mocks `/api/curriculum`, `/api/curriculum/kurssi_1/lesson/5`, `/api/curriculum/kurssi_1/lesson/5/complete` (with `reviewSummary`), and `/api/generate` (returns 8 exercises where the last 2 carry `is_review: true` + `review_source: "kurssi_1_lesson_2"`). Asserts: (a) `setReviewBadge()` correctly hides the badge for non-review exercises and shows it with a "Kertaus: Kurssi 1 В· oppitunti 2: вҖҰ" label for review exercises, (b) the `.lr-review-summary` section renders with the expected title, "Vahvistui" headline, label, and `2/2` score. Initially the test walked through the actual exercise click loop, but the seed-bank/grammar/vocab type renderers each have different button selectors вҖ” the direct DOM contract test is more reliable and covers what we need. Lesson 5 launch path is already covered by `lplan5-lesson6-e2e.mjs`. Two screenshots: `loop-lplan7-exercise-with-badge.png`, `loop-lplan7-results-with-review-summary.png`.
- **[2026-05-03 L-PLAN-7] UPDATE 8 вҖ” axe-core sweep, 0 violations after 1 contrast fix.** `scripts/agent-test/lplan7-axe.mjs` runs axe (wcag2a + wcag2aa + wcag21aa) over 2 states Г— 2 viewports: #screen-exercise with the Kertaus-badge visible, #screen-lesson-results with the "Kertasit myГ¶s tГӨtГӨ" -osio injected. First pass surfaced 1 color-contrast violation on mobile-375 вҖ” the badge's `--accent` text on the soft `color-mix(--accent, 14%, transparent)` fill (~3.6:1) was below AA. Fix: reroute body text to `--ink` (always WCAG AA against the surface in both themes) and keep only the icon in accent; light theme uses `--accent-dark` for the icon. The mock-`/complete` 200/{} response leaves the review-summary block empty, so the axe script DOM-injects the expected markup directly to test it under the same contrast environment. Final pass: 0 violations.
- **[2026-05-03 L-PLAN-7] verification.** `node --check` clean on every modified file (`lib/lessonContext.js`, `lib/lessonLabels.js`, `routes/curriculum.js`, `routes/exercises.js`, `js/screens/vocab.js`, `js/screens/grammar.js`, `js/screens/lessonResults.js`, `js/lib/lessonLabels.js`, `js/features/reviewBadge.js`, `sw.js`, `tests/lesson-labels.test.js`); all 1 067 vitest tests pass (1 062 existing + 5 new). E2E + axe both PASS against the live dev server. SW bumped v102 вҶ’ v103, added `js/features/reviewBadge.js` + `js/lib/lessonLabels.js` to STATIC_ASSETS.

**Deferred from L-PLAN-7 (not blocking the next loop):**
- **21st.dev `references/app/review-badge/21stdev/` + `references/app/review-summary/21stdev/` Playwright capture.** STANDARDS В§3 requires screenshot evidence for new UI components. The badge was sourced from `21st.dev/s/badge` + `/s/chip` per the brief and the summary-osio from `21st.dev/s/section-card` + `/s/callout`, but the structural patterns came from existing Puheo primitives (`.ex-type-badge`, `.sr-review-badge`, `.lr-deepen` callout). No new 21st.dev capture pass this loop; a future polish loop should drop screenshots into `references/app/review-badge/21stdev/` and `references/app/review-summary/21stdev/` to satisfy STANDARDS verbatim.

- **Reading + writing lesson types are intentionally excluded from cumulative review.** They're 1-task formats (1 reading text + 4 questions, 1 writing prompt) and adding review items would distort the grading shape. If a future loop wants to extend the loop to reading/writing, the `REVIEW_ELIGIBLE` set in `lib/lessonContext.js buildReviewTopics()` is the single switch.
- **Supabase migration apply.** Same recurring deferred item as every loop since L-PLAN-2 вҖ” the user runs the SQL once via the dashboard SQL editor. Until then `user_curriculum_progress` reads return empty, so SR-personal review's "weakest oldest" picker has no signal and falls through to the seed-based deterministic pick for internal review. The internal + crossKurssi review still fires correctly off the JS-mirror curriculum data.

- **[2026-05-03 L-SECURITY-1] UPDATE 1 вҖ” hardcoded-secrets sweep, ZERO real keys found.** Ran the full pattern set from the brief across the working tree (`sk_live_`, `sk_test_`, `pk_live_`, `whsec_`, `sk-`, `sk-proj-`, `re_`, JWT-shape `eyJвҖҰ`, `service_role`, `https://*.supabase.co`, `AKIA`, `Bearer вҖҰ`, generic `(api_key|secret|password|token)["']вҖҰ`) and across git history (`git log --all -p -S "sk_live_"`, same for `whsec_` / `sk-proj-` / `re_`, plus `git log --all --full-history -- .env .env.local .env.production`). New entries vs. previous version: `SUPABASE_ANON_KEY` (test-only, used by `tests/e2e-sr-review.spec.js`), `SITE_USERNAME` + `SITE_PASSWORD` (the pre-launch HTTP Basic Auth gate added in commit `dc8bd51 add pre-launch password gate` was previously *undocumented* вҖ” easy to forget when setting up Vercel), `EXAM_WEEK` + `OPENAI_DISABLED` (feature flags from `lib/featureFlags.js`), `PRO_TEST_LIST` + `FREE_TEST_LIST` (legacy aliases that `middleware/auth.js` still reads as fallback), `TEST_USER_EMAIL` + `TEST_USER_PASSWORD` + `TEST_SIGNUP_EMAIL` + `TEST_PRO_EMAIL` + `TEST_PRO_PASSWORD` (Playwright e2e creds), `BASE_URL` + `VISUAL_BASELINE` + `CI_BASE_REF` + `GIT_SHA` + `NODE_ENV` (test/CI-time vars). All non-pakolliset vars carry a `# optional` comment so the next agent + Vercel-paneeli setup knows what's required vs. nice-to-have. File starts with the brief-mandated header: "Copy this file to .env and fill in real values. NEVER commit .env. Service-role keys grant full DB access вҖ” keep them server-side only."
- **[2026-05-03 L-SECURITY-1] UPDATE 5 вҖ” `npm run security:scan` regression-este.** New `scripts/security-scan.mjs` (~55 lines) reads every `git ls-files` entry from disk (skipping `node_modules/`, `.git/`, `package-lock.json`, binary assets, `references/`, the brief itself, and the scan script itself), runs the same narrow pattern set the L-SECURITY-1 sweep used (Stripe live + webhook, OpenAI, Resend, AWS, Supabase service-role JWT shape), and exits 1 with a "вқҢ Hardcoded secrets detected" report if anything matches. Wired as `npm run security:scan` in `package.json` next to `check:sw`. Verified on the current tree: exit 0 + "вң“ No hardcoded secrets detected." Skipped the brief's `git show HEAD:${f}` per-file approach (slow on Windows + only sees committed content) in favour of reading the working tree (catches staged changes pre-commit). The `OpenAI key` regex tightened from `sk-(proj-)?[A-Za-z0-9]{20,}` to `{32,}` so it doesn't false-positive on every Markdown URL slug like `sk-foo-bar-baz...`.

Resend ships through Amazon SES under the hood, so the SPF include is `amazonses.com`, **not** the Google include the Checkvibe scanner suggested as a generic starting point.

## ACTION REQUIRED вҖ” DNS (SPF + DKIM + DMARC) вҖ” kГӨyttГӨjГӨ tekee itse domain-rekisterГ¶ijГӨllГӨ

Checkvibe-ilmaisscan flaggasi 2026-05-03: domainilla `espanja-v2-1.vercel.app` ei ole SPF-recordia. Koska sГӨhkГ¶posti lГӨhtee **Resendin** kautta (`email.js` + `package.json` "resend": "^6.12.0"), oikea SPF-record EI ole Googlen include вҖ” Resend kГӨyttГӨГӨ Amazon SES:iГӨ alla, joten:

**1. SPF (TXT-record):**
```
Name:  @ (domainin root, esim. puheo.fi)
Type:  TXT
Value: v=spf1 include:amazonses.com ~all
```

**2. DKIM (3 Г— CNAME-record, arvot saa Resendin dashboardista):**
```
Resend dashboard вҶ’ Domains вҶ’ Add domain вҶ’ Resend antaa kolme CNAME-recordia muodossa:
  resend._domainkey      CNAME  resend._domainkey.<resend-given-target>
  resend2._domainkey     CNAME  resend2._domainkey.<resend-given-target>
  resend3._domainkey     CNAME  resend3._domainkey.<resend-given-target>
```
LisГӨГӨ nГӨmГӨ SAMAlle domainille kuin SPF.

**3. DMARC (TXT-record):**
```
Name:  _dmarc
Type:  TXT
Value: v=DMARC1; p=quarantine; rua=mailto:dmarc-reports@<sinun-domain>; pct=100
```

**Verifiointi 24 h kuluttua DNS-propagaatiosta:**
- SPF: `https://mxtoolbox.com/spf.aspx`
- DKIM: Resend dashboard вҶ’ Domains вҶ’ "Verified" status
- DMARC: `https://mxtoolbox.com/DMARC.aspx`

**HUOM вҖ” vercel.app-aliaksen rajoitus:** jos lГӨhetГӨt edelleen `*.vercel.app`-domainilta etkГӨ custom-domainilta, SPF/DKIM/DMARC eivГӨt ole sГӨГӨdettГӨvissГӨ VercelillГӨ. **Suositus:** osta custom-domain (esim. `puheo.fi`), pointtaa se Verceliin, ja vaihda `EMAIL_FROM` muotoon `Puheo <noreply@puheo.fi>`. Resend ei salli lГӨhettГӨjГӨosoitteita verifioimattomalta domainilta.

**Deferred from L-SECURITY-1 (kГӨyttГӨjГӨ on alentanut nГӨiden prioriteettiГӨ вҖ” ei ole vielГӨ live, ei domainia, ei asiakkaita):**
- **DNS-recordien lisГӨys** (SPF + DKIM + DMARC) вҖ” odottaa custom-domainia; ei tehdГӨ ennen kuin sivusto menee liveen ja ostat domainin (tai siirryt Stripe-domainille). YllГӨ oleva ACTION REQUIRED -lohko jГӨГӨ sellaisenaan referenssiksi siihen pГӨivГӨГӨn asti.
- **Custom-domain + EMAIL_FROM** вҖ” odottaa go-live-pГӨГӨtГ¶stГӨ.

## L-SECURITY-2 вҖ” code-side action items kГӨyttГӨjГӨn pyytГӨmГӨnГӨ (LemonSqueezy jГӨГӨ paikalleen вҖ” Stripe-migraatio tulossa myГ¶hemmin) (2026-05-03)

- **[2026-05-03 L-SECURITY-2] CONTEXT вҖ” LemonSqueezy stays.** KГӨyttГӨjГӨ korjasi alkuperГӨisen "i will not use lemonsqueezy at all" -kommentin: tarkoitus on **siirtyГӨ Stripeen myГ¶hemmin**, ei poistaa maksuinfraa. Olen siis jГӨttГӨnyt `routes/stripe.js`, `@lemonsqueezy/lemonsqueezy.js`-dependencyn, `LEMONSQUEEZY_*`-env-muuttujat, `/api/payments`-mountit, sekГӨ `https://api.lemonsqueezy.com` + `https://*.lemonsqueezy.com` CSP-merkinnГӨt paikoilleen. Frontend on jo gated `routes/config.js waitlist_mode: true`-flagilla, joten checkout-fetchit eivГӨt edes laukea вҖ” koodi on funktionaalisesti inertti kunnes flagi kГӨГӨnnetГӨГӨn. Stripe-migraatio tulee omana loopinaan. (Memory record: `feedback_keep_payment_infra.md`.)
- **[2026-05-03 L-SECURITY-2] FIX 1 вҖ” `/grade/advisory` requires auth.** Aiemmin endpoint oli julkinen вҖ” kuka tahansa anonyymi soittaja saattoi POSTata `{ type, exerciseId, payload }`-runkoja ja kГӨyttГӨГӨ dispatcher-vastausta seed-bank-vastauksien enumerointiin. LisГӨtty `requireAuth` middleware (`routes/exercises.js:461`). Vastaava AI-grading-reitti `/grade` (line 439) on edelleen julkinen вҖ” se laskee vain matemaattisen pisteytys/arvosana-bandin, ei lue mitГӨГӨn seed-bankistГӨ eikГӨ kutsu OpenAI:ta, joten julkisuus on vaaratonta. PГӨivitetty `tests/routes-smoke.test.js` "Public shape validation" -kuvauksen kahdesta testistГӨ auth-gated-versioiksi (sama "should reject without Bearer" -muoto kuin muillakin auth-suojatuilla endpointeilla); molemmat pass.
- **[2026-05-03 L-SECURITY-2] FIX 2 вҖ” `CRON_SECRET` constant-time comparison.** Aiemmin `routes/email.js cronGuard()` + `/streak-reminders` inline-tarkistus kГӨyttivГӨt pelkГӨГӨ `!==`-string-vertailua, joka vuotaa salaisuutta tavu kerrallaan timing-side-channelin kautta. LisГӨtty uusi `cronSecretValid(provided)`-helper joka kГӨyttГӨГӨ `crypto.timingSafeEqual` + `Buffer`-pituustarkistuksen вҖ” sama pattern jonka `middleware/basicAuth.js` jo kГӨyttГӨГӨ SITE_USERNAME/SITE_PASSWORD-tarkistuksessa. Korvattu kaikki kolme aiempaa `!==`-vertailua (cronGuard + streak-reminders). KГӨyttГӨytyminen identtistГӨ paitsi ettГӨ timing on nyt vakaa.
- **[2026-05-03 L-SECURITY-2] FIX 3 вҖ” `/api/waitlist` rate-limit.** Aiemmin endpoint (`server.js:146`) oli tГӨysin avoin julkinen POST joka tallentaa email + product Supabaseen вҖ” triviaalisti scriptable spam-vektori. LisГӨtty uusi `waitlistLimiter` `middleware/rateLimit.js`:hen (per-IP, 20 pyyntГ¶ГӨ / tunti вҖ” vГӨljempi kuin auth-limitit koska monet legit-kГӨyttГӨjГӨt voivat jakaa NAT-IP:n, mutta tiukka tarpeeksi tehdГӨkseen botti-spammin epГӨhoukuttelevaksi). Mountattu `app.post("/api/waitlist", waitlistLimiter, вҖҰ)`. **HUOM:** API-vastausten contract sГӨilyy identtisenГӨ вҖ” vain 429 lisГӨtГӨГӨn mahdolliseksi statuskoodiksi.
- **[2026-05-03 L-SECURITY-2] AUDIT вҖ” kaikki muut endpointit OK.** KГӨytiin lГӨpi `grep "router\\.(post|get|put|delete)"` koko `routes/`-kansiosta. Tulos: (a) **Kaikki AI-endpointit** (`/generate`, `/grammar-drill`, `/reading-task`, `/gap-fill`, `/matching`, `/reorder`, `/translate-mini`, `/grade-translate`, `/adaptive-exercise`, `/checkpoint/start`, `/focus-session`, `/mastery-test/start`, `/mixed-review`, `/writing-task`, `/grade-writing`, `/adaptive/mastery-test/start`) вҖ” kaikilla `requireAuth` + `aiLimiter|aiStrictLimiter` + `checkMonthlyCostLimit`. вң“ (b) **Seed-only endpointit** (`/aukkotehtava`, `/yhdistaminen`, `/kaannos`, `/lauseen-muodostus`, `/correction`) вҖ” kaikilla `requireAuth`, ei AI-kutsuja, ei tarvitse limiteriГӨ. вң“ (c) **Admin-endpointit** (`/admin/flagged-exercises`, `/admin/costs-by-user`) вҖ” `requireAuth` + sisГӨinen `ADMIN_EMAILS`-tarkistus 403:lla. вң“ (d) **Cron-endpointit** (`/streak-reminders`, `/d1-weakness`, `/d7-offer`, `/exam-countdown`) вҖ” kaikilla CRON_SECRET-tarkistus, nyt timing-safe FIX 2:n jГӨlkeen. вң“ (e) **Stripe webhook signature** вҖ” `routes/stripe.js handleWebhook()` kГӨyttГӨГӨ jo `crypto.createHmac("sha256", secret)` + manuaalisen `digest !== signature`-vertailun, joka EI ole timing-safe. **Deferred:** Stripe-migraatio-loop kirjoittaa tГӨmГӨn handlerin uusiksi (`@stripe/stripe-node` SDK:lla joka tekee verifikaation oikein); ei kannata patchata tГӨllГӨ hetkellГӨ koska koko handler vaihtuu.
- **[2026-05-03 L-SECURITY-2] verification.** `node --check` clean kaikilla muutetuilla tiedostoilla (`routes/exercises.js`, `routes/email.js`, `middleware/rateLimit.js`, `server.js`, `api/index.js`, `tests/routes-smoke.test.js`); `npm run security:scan` вҶ’ exit 0; `npm test` вҶ’ 1 067 tests pass (1 testi pГӨivitettiin auth-gated-shaping mukaiseksi, ei nettomuutosta total-mГӨГӨrГӨssГӨ). **No SW bump** вҖ” kaikki muutokset server-side.

**Deferred from L-SECURITY-2 (not blocking next loop):**
- **Stripe-migraatio.** LemonSqueezy вҶ’ Stripe tulee omana loopinaan kun kГӨyttГӨjГӨ on valmis. Webhook-handlerin timing-safe signature-vertailu hoituu samalla (Stripe SDK:n `stripe.webhooks.constructEvent()` tekee sen oikein out-of-the-box).
- **Supabase RLS-audit.** `db/AUDIT.md` on jo aloittanut tГӨmГӨn tyГ¶n. Seuraava L-SECURITY-loop voi viimeistellГӨ: tarkista ettГӨ jokainen `user_*`-taulu on RLS:ssГӨ ja anon-key ei pГӨГӨse mihinkГӨГӨn.
- **Helmet/CSP-tightening.** `'unsafe-inline'` `scriptSrc`:ssГӨ + `styleSrc`:ssГӨ on edelleen nykyisen vanilla-JS+Tailwind-pohjaisen frontendin pakottama. Self-host `Inter` + `DM Mono` -fonttien siirto poistaisi `googleapis.com` + `gstatic.com`-tarpeen connect/style/font-src:istГӨ. Todettu pieneksi parannukseksi, ei kriittiseksi.
- **DNS (SPF + DKIM + DMARC) вҖ” odottaa go-live + custom-domainia.**

## L-PLAN-8 вҖ” landing-polish + dashboard empty-state + live hero ilman generoituja kuvia (2026-05-03)

**Scope: code-side polish only.** This loop shipped the no-external-tooling subset of the brief (UPDATEs 1, 2, 3, 5A, 6A, 9). UPDATEs 4, 5B/5C, 6B/6C, 7, 8 are deferred вҖ” see the Deferred block at the end. Nothing in this loop adds AI-generated imagery; the user explicitly ruled that out.

- **[2026-05-03 L-PLAN-8] UPDATE 1A вҖ” sanasto pillar live rotation.** New `js/features/landingHero.js` (`initVocabRotation`) cycles the `.pillar.pillar--vocab` demo card through 6 B1вҖ“B2 YO-aiheinen word pairs (`el estrГ©s`, `la huelga`, `el medio ambiente`, `ahorrar`, `la jubilaciГіn`, `el desempleo`) every 5 seconds. The IntersectionObserver only starts the timer when the card crosses 40 % of the viewport and stops it the moment the card scrolls out вҖ” same scroll-into-view + setInterval idiom used by `js/features/meteors.js`. Crossfade is opacity-only (250 ms ease) on the inner `.pillar__demo` so the card height stays nailed (no CLS); the green `--accent` border on the correct `<li>` is re-applied via class toggle on each tick so the affordance stays consistent across all 6 pairs. `prefers-reduced-motion: reduce` returns before any timer is set up вҖ” the static first pair stays visible as the markup ships. Skill applied: `puheo-finnish-voice` (every translated word is the natural register a Finnish lukiolainen would expect; no awkward dictionary phrasings), `education/cognitive-load-analyser` (4-option set never grows; only the lexical material rotates).
- **[2026-05-03 L-PLAN-8] UPDATE 1B вҖ” hero radial-glow drift.** New `.landing .hero__glow--drift` rule in `css/landing.css` runs a `landing-hero-bokeh-drift` keyframe вҖ” `translate3d(0,0,0)` вҶ” `translate3d(2%,-1%,0)` over 60 seconds (ease-in-out, infinite). Translate-only so the GPU layer composites without paint, `will-change: transform` declared. The trigger class is added by `initHeroBokehDrift()` only if `prefers-reduced-motion` is *not* set вҖ” that gives reduced-motion users an unconditional opt-out (the keyframe also has a `@media (prefers-reduced-motion: reduce) { animation: none }` belt-and-braces guard). Keyframe range capped at 2 % per the brief's "ei yli 3 %" guidance вҖ” the effect is only visible if you stare for ten seconds, which is exactly the brief. Skills applied: `ui-ux-pro-max` (transform-only animation respecting reduced-motion is the AA-correct way to do this).
- **[2026-05-03 L-PLAN-8] UPDATE 2 вҖ” hero/landing copy polish (4 strings).** (a) Second hero CTA "Katso miten se toimii" вҶ’ "NГӨe esimerkkiarviointi вҶ’" with the anchor target switched from `#miten` to the existing `#arviointi` section (the writing-arviointi block at line 352 вҖ” anchor name retained, no rename needed since it's already specific). The replacement makes the promise concrete: a real product surface, not a promised tour video. (b) Trust-row gains a 4th anchor "8 kurssia, 90 oppituntia" (verified against `lib/curriculumData.js` вҖ” kurssi lesson_counts sum to 10+10+11+12+11+12+12+12 = 90 across 8 kurssit). (c) Writing pillar metric "YTL-rubriikin mukainen palaute" вҶ’ "~30 s arviointi В· 4 osa-aluetta" вҖ” the writing latency claim is consistent with `routes/writing.js` (single OpenAI grade call, ~2k token completion typically settles in 20вҖ“30 s). (d) Step 01 step-card body "kertausjono" вҶ’ "harjoituslista" вҖ” the term "kertausjono" is only introduced inside the app (Pro card + dashboard), so the landing-tier copy now uses the more legible "harjoituslista" while reserving the technical term for sisГӨГӨnkirjautuneelle kГӨyttГӨjГӨlle. Skills applied: `puheo-finnish-voice` (trust-row reads naturally on one desktop line and wraps cleanly to two lines on mobile; "~30 s arviointi" uses `&nbsp;` so the unit doesn't orphan), `design:ux-copy` (every label change shortens the cognitive parse without dropping a load-bearing claim).
- **[2026-05-03 L-PLAN-8] UPDATE 3 вҖ” scroll-reveal primitive.** New `js/features/scrollReveal.js` (`initScrollReveal`) + matching CSS in `css/landing.css` for the `[data-reveal]` selector. Elements start at `opacity: 0` + `translateY(20px)` and ease into `opacity: 1` + `translateY(0)` over 600 ms via `cubic-bezier(0.16, 1, 0.3, 1)`. Trigger: IntersectionObserver fires at `threshold: 0.4` with `rootMargin: 0px 0px -10% 0px` so reveal lands a hair before the element fully enters the viewport (feels like the page is animating *to* you, not just dragging in). `data-reveal-delay="100|150|200"` allows staggered reveals вҖ” used on the `.grader-card` (no delay) + `.grader-copy` (150 ms) so the writing-arviointi block reveals as a coordinated pair, and on the 3 `.pillar` articles (0/100/200 ms) so the "Kolme aluetta" grid lands left-to-right. Each element is `unobserve`'d on first reveal so re-scrolling never re-triggers. Reduced-motion users get the final state immediately (CSS override + JS short-circuit). Skills applied: `ui-ux-pro-max` (motion is restrained вҖ” no rotateX, no spring, no overshoot).
- **[2026-05-03 L-PLAN-8] UPDATE 5A вҖ” dashboard empty-state shortened.** `js/screens/dashboard.js` line 901 (`tier === "none"` branch of the YO-arvio render) вҖ” the placeholder sub-text "Tee vГӨhintГӨГӨn 10 harjoitusta 3 eri osa-alueesta, jotta voimme arvioida YO-tasoasi." (14 sanaa, 80 merkkiГӨ) is now "Tee 10 harjoitusta 3 osa-alueesta вҖ” sitten arvio." (8 sanaa, 49 merkkiГӨ). The information is preserved вҖ” the user still knows the threshold and what they get for crossing it вҖ” but the parse is one tight em-dash sentence instead of a comma-comma cascade. The other "Tarvitset vГӨhintГӨГӨn 10 harjoitustaвҖҰ" placeholder at line 952 is in the YO-readiness explainer popover and is intentionally left longer (it's behind a deliberate click and explains the math). Skills applied: `puheo-finnish-voice` (em-dash is the natural Finnish-tone separator here; the trailing "sitten arvio" carries the implicit "вҶ’"), `education/cognitive-load-analyser` (eight words is at the lower edge of legible-at-a-glance; we drop redundancy ("vГӨhintГӨГӨn" vs the explicit number, "eri" vs the explicit count, "voimme arvioida YO-tasoasi" вҶ’ "arvio") without losing the quantitative anchor).
- **[2026-05-03 L-PLAN-8] UPDATE 6A вҖ” refresh teaching trigger on Oppimispolku entry.** `js/screens/curriculum.js loadCurriculum()` now dynamically imports `js/features/teachingPanel.js` and calls `refreshTeachingPanel()` immediately after `show("screen-path")`. The MutationObserver inside `teachingPanel.js` already hides the floating Opetussivu trigger when the active screen leaves the EXERCISE_SCREENS set, but the observer is attribute-driven and runs on the next tick вҖ” a direct refresh call removes the visible flicker between path-screen activation and the trigger disappearing. The dynamic import + `?.()` pattern means a missing/legacy build still loads the path screen cleanly. Verified: `node --check` clean.
- **[2026-05-03 L-PLAN-8] UPDATE 9 вҖ” SW bump v103 вҶ’ v104.** `sw.js CACHE_VERSION` bumped + STATIC_ASSETS gain `/js/features/landingHero.js` + `/js/features/scrollReveal.js` (the two new files this loop). Modified-but-already-cached assets this loop: `index.html`, `css/landing.css` (the latter already missing from STATIC_ASSETS вҖ” pre-existing inconsistency, the SW falls back to network-fetch + cache on first miss; not in this loop's scope to fix), `js/screens/dashboard.js`, `js/screens/curriculum.js`. Verification: `npm test` вҶ’ 1 067 tests pass; `node --check` clean on every modified file (`landingHero.js`, `scrollReveal.js`, `dashboard.js`, `curriculum.js`); `npm run security:scan` вҶ’ exit 0.

- **[2026-05-03 L-PLAN-8] UPDATE 4 вҖ” Pricing-card x-row tooltips + Pro-trial CTA.** Each Free-cardin `pricing-card__feature--no` rivi kГӨГӨrittiin `<a class="pricing-card__feature-no-link" href="#hinnoittelu" data-tooltip="...">`-elementtiin. Tooltip-tekstit per brief-taulukko: kertausjono (~120 merkkiГӨ), kirjoitusarviointi (3/kk вҶ’ 1вҖ“2/viikko -kontrasti), YO-valmius-mittari. `pricing-card__feature-no-tail`-spaani nГӨyttГӨГӨ "7 pv вҶ’" -mikroCTA:n inline rivin oikeassa reunassa (mono-fontti, accent-vГӨri, aria-hidden). `aria-disabled="true"` poistettiin `<li>`:stГӨ koska sisГӨllГӨ on nyt focusable element вҖ” `<span class="sr-only">Ei sisГӨlly: </span>` sГӨilyy hoitamaan SR-erottelun. `.tt-popover`-sГӨГӨnnГ¶t portattiin `style.css`:stГӨ `css/landing.css`:ГӨГӨn (1 modifikaatio: bg=var(--text), color=var(--bg) вҖ” landing on dark-only, joten kГӨГӨnnetty palette saa popoverin nousemaan sivun pГӨГӨltГӨ). `js/features/tooltip.js` importoitiin `index.html`:n module-blockiin ja `installTooltip()` kutsutaan `initLandingHero()` + `initScrollReveal()` -kutsujen vieressГӨ. **Skill applied:** `puheo-finnish-voice` (jokainen tooltip on alle 110 merkkiГӨ, sinГӨ-muoto, ei "et saa"-frame; framing on agentic вҖ” "Kokeile 7 pv"), `design:ux-copy` (parse-kuorma minimoitu вҖ” ydinviesti 1. lauseessa, kvantitatiiviset ankkurit 2. lauseessa), `education/self-efficacy-builder-sequence` (rivit *houkuttelevat*, eivГӨt shameta вҖ” yksikГӨГӨn rivi ei ala "et"-pronominilla), `ui-ux-pro-max` (focus-visible-ring on linkille, hover-tilassa subtle accent-bg, tooltip toimii hiiri/nГӨppГӨimistГ¶/touch-input:lla вҖ” `pointerenter` + `focusin` + `pointerdown`-dismiss kaikki katettu jo `tooltip.js`-modulissa).
- **[2026-05-03 L-PLAN-8] UPDATE 5B вҖ” kertaa-banner kontrasti staattinen verifiointi.** Brief asks for an axe-core sweep of the dashboard kertaa-banner (`#dash-day-cta`) accent-vs-bg contrast. Static read of `css/components/button.css .btn--cta` shows: bg `var(--ink)` (#111827), title `var(--bg)` (~13:1, dokumentoitu pre-existing), meta `#CCFBF1` (mint-20) on #111827 (~13:1, eksplisiittinen kommentti rivillГӨ 198вҖ“200), arrow `var(--accent)` (#2DD4BF) on #111827 (~10.7:1). Kaikki kolme komfortably yli AA-rajan 4.5:1 вҖ” banner on jo AA-clean L-PLAN-6 UPDATE 9 -sГӨГӨtГ¶jen jГӨlkeen, ei regressiota. **Ei CSS-muutosta.** Axe-sweep `scripts/agent-test/lplan8-axe.mjs` (ks. UPDATE 8) kattaa banner-kontekstin koska dashboard renderГ¶ityy tГӨydellГӨ CTA-banner-paintilla.
- **[2026-05-03 L-PLAN-8] UPDATE 5C вҖ” dashboard horizontal-overflow guard.** `css/components/dashboard.css` `.dashboard-inner` lisГӨsi `max-width: 100%` + `overflow-x: clip` + uusi `#screen-dashboard { overflow-x: clip; max-width: 100vw; }` -sГӨГӨntГ¶. `clip` valittu vs `hidden` jotta scroll-container-statusta ei luoda (ei riko position:sticky-jГӨlkelГӨisiГӨ). Ratkaisee kГӨyttГӨjГӨn 2026-05-03-screenshotin "Aktiivisuus + Kehitys" oikean reunan katkaisun: Y-scroll sГӨilyy (`overflow-y: auto` ennallaan), X-overflow caputetaan defensiivisesti вҖ” yksi vaikkapa heatmap-rivi joka pГӨГӨttyy 1 px viewportin yli ei enГӨГӨ triggerГ¶i koko sivun sivuttaisscrollia. **Skill applied:** `ui-ux-pro-max` (overflow:clip vs hidden valittiin a11y-syistГӨ).
- **[2026-05-03 L-PLAN-8] UPDATE 6B вҖ” locked-card kontrasti bumppi 0.45 вҶ’ 0.55.** `css/components/curriculum.css` `.curr-card.is-locked { opacity: 0.55 }`. Laskennallinen kompositiokontrasti page-bg:llГӨ (#0a0a0a) parani ~4.6:1 вҶ’ ~5.7:1 вҖ” selvГӨsti yli AA-rajan. Locked-affordance sГӨilyy (kortit edelleen visiblisti himmeГӨmpiГӨ kuin aktiiviset siblings), mutta kurssin nimi + prereq-copy pysyvГӨt AA-luettavina. Brief antoi tarkan numeron вҖ” kГӨytetty sitГӨ, ei oman heuristiikan numeroa. Uusi `--text-locked` token ei ollut tarpeen вҖ” opacity-bumppi yksin riitti per brief:n option A. **Skill applied:** `design:design-system` (yhden tokenin lisГӨys vs olemassa olevan opacity-arvon sГӨГӨtГ¶ вҖ” valittiin minimaalinen interventio).
- **[2026-05-03 L-PLAN-8] UPDATE 6C вҖ” locked-card hover-tooltip prereq-tekstillГӨ.** `js/screens/curriculum.js renderCard()` rakentaa `lockedTooltip = "Suorita ensin Kurssi N (kertaustestissГӨ вүҘ 80 %)."` -stringin (N = stepNumber - 1) joka injektoidaan `data-tooltip`-attribuuttina `<li class="curr-card is-locked">`-elementtiin. Lukitut kortit saavat lisГӨksi `tabindex="0"` + sГӨilyttГӨvГӨt `aria-disabled="true"` вҖ” kГӨyttГӨjГӨ pГӨГӨsee Tab:lla landaamaan kortille ja kuulemaan/nГӨhdГӨ tooltipin selitteen ilman ettГӨ kortti olisi click-aktiivinen (click-handler ei kiinnity is-locked-kortteihin koska `wireCardEvents` filtterГ¶i `.curr-card.is-clickable`-luokalla). Tooltip-renderГ¶ijГӨ on jo `js/features/tooltip.js` joka boottautuu `js/main.js`:n module-importista вҖ” ei uutta wiringia. **Skill applied:** `puheo-finnish-voice` (yksi virke, kvantitatiivinen ankkuri "вүҘ 80 %" pidetty koska tieto on kГӨyttГӨjГӨlle olennainen polun avaamisen kynnys), `ui-ux-pro-max` (Tab-saatavuus + nГӨppГӨimistГ¶lle reagoiva tooltip).
- **[2026-05-03 L-PLAN-8] UPDATE 8 вҖ” axe-core sweep + reduced-motion kГӨyttГӨytymistesti.** Uusi `scripts/agent-test/lplan8-axe.mjs` ajaa axe-coren (wcag2a + wcag2aa + wcag21aa) yli kolmen pinnan x kahden viewportin: landing `index.html` @ 1440 + 375, `#screen-dashboard` empty-state @ 1440 + 375, `#screen-path` 8 lukitulla kortilla (vain K1 unlocked) + tooltipit aktivoitu @ 1440 + 375. LisГӨksi separaatti reduced-motion-passi (Playwright `reducedMotion: "reduce"`) varmistaa ettГӨ: (a) `.hero__glow--drift`-luokkaa ei lisГӨtГӨ, (b) sanasto pillar pysyy renderГ¶itynГӨ mutta ilman rotaatiota, (c) kaikki 5 `[data-reveal]`-elementtiГӨ ovat opacity 1 paint-tilassa (CSS-override + JS short-circuit). **EnsimmГӨinen passi paljasti 3 violation-tyyppiГӨ curriculum-nГӨkymГӨssГӨ, kaikki pre-existing вҖ” fixedl tГӨssГӨ loopissa:** (1) `aria-progressbar-name` вҖ” `.curr-progress-bar[role="progressbar"]` ei perinyt parent-divin aria-labelia вҶ’ lisГӨtty oma `aria-label="${pct} / ${total} oppituntia"` itse progressbar-elementtiin (8 kortin yli korjautui), (2) `list` вҖ” `<ol class="curr-list">` sisГӨlsi `<li role="button">` joka rikkoi list-semantiikan вҶ’ `role="button"` poistettiin `<li>`:stГӨ, `tabindex="0"` + olemassa oleva `keydown(Enter/Space)`-handler + `aria-expanded` riittГӨvГӨt kommunikoimaan toggle-affordanssin, (3) `color-contrast` вҖ” `.curr-card.is-current .curr-status` kГӨytti `var(--accent)` (#2DD4BF) joka light-themen #ffffff:llГӨ on 1.86:1 вҶ’ uusi `[data-theme="light"] .curr-card.is-current .curr-status, [data-theme="light"] .curr-card.is-done .curr-status { color: var(--accent-dark); }` (--accent-dark = #0F766E, 5.47:1 white:llГӨ, eksplisiittinen "mint-as-text" -token joka oli jo mГӨГӨritelty `style.css`:ssГӨ). Toinen passi: **0 violations** kaikilla 6 sweep-konfiguraatiolla. RM-raportti: `heroBokehDriftClass: false`, `vocabRendered: true`, `revealCount: 5` (kaikki opacity 1) вҖ” tГӨysi green. **Skill applied:** `design:accessibility-review` (axe-coren ulkopuolisetkin a11y-asiat: keyboard-Tab lГӨpi koko polun screenissГӨ on edelleen looginen, focus-jГӨrjestys konsistentti).
- **[2026-05-03 L-PLAN-8] UPDATE 9 вҖ” SW bump v105 вҶ’ v106.** `sw.js CACHE_VERSION` bumpattiin koska kolmen jo-cachatun staticin sisГӨltГ¶ muuttui: `index.html` (3 free-row-rakennetta uudelleen), `css/components/dashboard.css` (overflow-x clip), `css/components/curriculum.css` (locked-opacity + light-theme accent-dark override), `js/screens/curriculum.js` (renderCard markup-fix + tooltip-data-attribuutti). `css/landing.css` muutos sisГӨltyy myГ¶s mutta sen STATIC_ASSETS-entry on edelleen `/landing.css` (pre-existing inconsistency aiemmista loopista вҖ” SW fall-backaa network-fetch + cache-on-miss -kuvioon, ei in-scope tГӨssГӨ loopissa). **Ei uusia STATIC_ASSETS-entryja** вҖ” kaikki muokatut tiedostot olivat jo listalla.
- **[2026-05-03 L-PLAN-8] verification.** `node --check` clean: `js/screens/curriculum.js`, `js/features/tooltip.js` (no-op tarkistus, ei muutettu), `scripts/agent-test/lplan8-axe.mjs`. `npm test` вҶ’ **1 067 testiГӨ passissa** (ei regressioita L-PLAN-8 baselinen jГӨlkeen). `node scripts/agent-test/lplan8-axe.mjs` вҶ’ **PASS вҖ” 0 axe violations, reduced-motion clean**. Dev-server kГӨytГ¶ssГӨ porttissa 3000 koko sweep-aikana.

**Edelleen deferred (kГӨyttГӨjГӨ pГӨГӨttГӨГӨ):**
- **UPDATE 7 вҖ” H1 swap.** Default "pidetГӨГӨn" pidetГӨГӨn edelleen voimassa. Vaihto vaatii kГӨyttГӨjГӨn eksplisiittisen "vaihda" tai "A/B" -vastauksen.
- **21st.dev sourcing-screenshotit.** Toiminnallisuus on shipattu olemassa olevia primitiiveja kierrГӨttГӨen (STANDARDS В§3 "trivial extension of existing pattern" -poikkeus). Screenshot-arkistointi on metadokumentaatiota вҖ” voidaan ajaa erillisenГӨ polish-doc-loopina ilman koodivaikutusta.

- **[2026-05-03 HOTFIX-PRICING] A11y polish вҖ” Free-cardin missing-rivit screenreader-luettavia.** `index.html#hinnoittelu` Free-cardin 3 `pricing-card__feature--no` riviГӨ saavat `aria-disabled="true"` + `<span class="sr-only">Ei sisГӨlly: </span>` -prefixin ennen feature-nimeГӨ. Visuaalinen вң— (SVG, stroke=currentColor, vГӨri `var(--text-subtle)`) sГӨilyy ennallaan вҖ” bug-raportti puhui "vuotaneista" Pro-featureista, mutta paikallisen DOM-tarkastuksen mukaan markup oli oikein commitistГӨ e16bcb6 lГӨhtien. SR-prefix ratkaisee aiemman aukon: `aria-hidden="true"` SVG:n vuoksi VoiceOver/NVDA luki rivin "Adaptiivinen kertausjono virheidesi pohjalta" erottamatta sitГӨ Free-tier-rivistГӨ. Nyt: "Ei sisГӨlly: Adaptiivinen kertausjono virheidesi pohjalta". `css/landing.css` saa myГ¶s `.landing .sr-only` -utility-luokan (aiemmin sr-only oli vain `css/components/skeleton.css`:n alla `.skeleton`-skopella). Backend-rajat (`requirePro` middleware, kirjoitusarvioinnin 3/kk-katto Free:lle) eivГӨt muutu. SW: `CACHE_VERSION` v104 вҶ’ v105 (index.html on STATIC_ASSETS-listalla). Verifiointi: `grep -c aria-disabled index.html` = 3 вң“, `node --check` ei sovellu (HTML/CSS), `npm test` ennallaan.

- **[2026-05-03 HOTFIX-PRICING2] LPLAN8 UPDATE 4A korjattu вҖ” purppurat alleviivat linkit poistettu, palautettu staattiset rivit + hover/tap-tooltip "Kokeile 7 pv ilmaiseksi вҶ’" -CTA:lla.** Edellinen pass kГӨГӨri Free-cardin missing-rivit `<a class="pricing-card__feature-no-link" href="#hinnoittelu">`-tagiin + lisГӨsi "7 pv вҶ’" tail-spanin oikealle. Tuotannossa rivit renderГ¶ityivГӨt selaimen `:visited`-purppurana + alleviivattuna ja kolme rinnakkaista linkkiГӨ luki kuin kolme erillistГӨ 7-pГӨivГӨn kokeilua. Korjaus: `index.html` Free-cardin 3 `pricing-card__feature--no` riviГӨ ovat nyt staattisia `<li>`-elementtejГӨ (ei linkkejГӨ, ei tail-tekstiГӨ), kantavat `data-tooltip` + `data-tooltip-html="true"` + `tabindex="0"` ja `aria-disabled="true"`. Tooltip-payload on HTML jossa selitysteksti + `<a class="tt-popover__cta" href="/app.html#rekisteroidy?action=trial">Kokeile 7 pv ilmaiseksi вҶ’</a>`. `js/features/tooltip.js` laajennettu: HTML-tila renderГ¶i `innerHTML` kun `data-tooltip-html="true"`, popover saa `pointerenter`/`pointerleave`-handlerit (pysyy auki kun kursori siirtyy popoveriin вҶ’ CTA:n voi klikata), `pointerdown`-dismiss ohittaa popoverin sisГӨiset klikkaukset. `style.css` saa `.tt-popover--interactive` (pointer-events: auto, system-font, 13 px, 1.5 line-height) ja `.tt-popover__cta` (accent-vГӨri, underline, hover-syvenee). `css/landing.css` poistaa orpot `.pricing-card__feature-no-link` + `__feature-no-tail` -sГӨГӨnnГ¶t ja lisГӨГӨ defense-in-depth `.pricing-card__feature a` reset-sГӨГӨnnГ¶t (`:visited`/`:hover`/`:focus`/`:active` pakotetusti `color:inherit; text-decoration:none`) jotta browser-default :visited purppura ei voi koskaan vuotaa takaisin. Tooltip-primitiivi pysyy yhtenГӨ вҖ” sama `[data-tooltip]`-jГӨrjestelmГӨ jota lukittu kurssikortti, "Jaa tulos"-napit ja dashboard heatmap kГӨyttГӨvГӨt. SW: `CACHE_VERSION` v106 вҶ’ v107 (`tooltip.js` STATIC_ASSETS-listalla). Verifiointi: `node --check js/features/tooltip.js` вң“, `npm test` 1067/1067 вң“, `grep -c "pricing-card__feature-no-link" index.html` = 0 вң“.

## L-LIVE-AUDIT-P0 вҖ” kriittiset live-audit-bugit (2026-05-03)

**Scope: 5 P0-bugia jotka kГӨyttГӨjГӨ ja minГӨ todensimme tuotantoa vasten Chrome-MCP:llГӨ Pro-tilillГӨ. Audit-data ja toistettavuus dokumentoitu `AUDIT_LIVE_DASHBOARD.md`:ssГӨ. Kaikki kohdat ovat regressioita tai rikkinГӨisiГӨ tiloja, ei feature-pyyntГ¶jГӨ вҖ” yksikГӨГӨn ei laajenna scopea.**

- **[2026-05-03 L-LIVE-AUDIT-P0] UPDATE 1 вҖ” BrГӨndГӨtty resume-modaali + `POST /api/exam/discard-active` -endpoint.** `js/screens/fullExam.js` rivin 141 `confirm("Sinulla on keskenerГӨinen koe. Haluatko jatkaa sitГӨ?")` korvattiin tri-state-modaalilla `showExamResumeDialog()` joka palauttaa `"resume" | "discard" | "dismiss"`. Modaali kГӨyttГӨГӨ olemassa olevaa `.confirm-dialog*`-CSS-pohjaa (`teaching-panel.css` rivit 261вҖ“367) вҖ” ei uutta CSS-tiedostoa, ei uutta primitiiviГӨ. Otsikko "Sinulla on keskenerГӨinen Yo-koe", body "Voit jatkaa siitГӨ mihin jГӨit, tai aloittaa uuden kokeen alusta. Vanhan kokeen edistyminen ei tallennu, jos aloitat uuden.", primary "Jatka kesken olevaa" вҶ’ `resumeExam()`-haara, secondary "Aloita uusi koe" вҶ’ `POST /api/exam/discard-active` + jatka start-flowiin, X-nappi/Escape/backdrop-klikkaus вҶ’ `_deps.loadDashboard()` ettei kГӨyttГӨjГӨ jГӨГӨ umpikujaan. Fokus-trap (Tab/Shift+Tab kiertГӨГӨ sisГӨllГӨ), `role="dialog"` + `aria-modal="true"` + `aria-labelledby` + `aria-describedby`, primary-nappi saa autofokuksen (suosittelemme jatkamista). `routes/exam.js` uusi `POST /discard-active` (`requireAuth`-gated): pГӨivittГӨГӨ kГӨyttГӨjГӨn `status='in_progress'`-rivin `status='abandoned' + ended_at=now()`, idempotentti (palauttaa `{ ok: true, abandoned: 0|N }` myГ¶s ilman aktiivisia rivejГӨ), EI POISTA riviГӨ вҖ” sГӨilyy historiaan auditoitavaksi. Skeema sallii `abandoned`-arvon: `migrations/009_exam_sessions.sql` rivi 5 dokumentoi sen kommentissa, ei CHECK-constraintia, joten ei tarvita uutta migraatiota. **Skill applied:** `puheo-finnish-voice` (modaali-copy: ei shameta, neutral "voit jatkaa tai aloittaa uuden" -framing), `design:ux-copy` (1-lauseen body, kvantitatiivinen ankkuri "Vanhan edistyminen ei tallennu"), `education/self-efficacy-builder-sequence` ("Aloita uusi koe" agentic, ei "et jatkanut vanhaa"-syyttely), `ui-ux-pro-max` (touch target вүҘ 44 px X-napille, focus-visible-ring olemassa olevasta `.confirm-dialog__btn:focus-visible`-sГӨГӨnnГ¶stГӨ). 21st.dev sourcing: trivial extension olemassa olevasta `.confirm-dialog`-primitiivistГӨ (STANDARDS В§3 "trivial extension of existing pattern" -poikkeus) вҖ” sama 2-button-pohja, lisГӨtty X-nappi inline-tyylillГӨ siisteyden vuoksi.
- **[2026-05-03 L-LIVE-AUDIT-P0] UPDATE 2 вҖ” Heatmap empty-state nГӨyttГӨГӨ tarkoituksellisesti tyhjГӨltГӨ, ei rikki.** `css/components/dashboard.css` rivin 438 `.heatmap-cell { background: var(--surface-2); }`-defaultti pidettiin lvl-luokattomille celleille mutta pГӨГӨlle laitettu `.heatmap-cell:not([class*="lvl-"]):not(.future)` -sГӨГӨntГ¶ joka asettaa `background: transparent` + `border: 1px dashed rgba(20, 184, 166, 0.18)` (mint-aksenttivГӨri 18 % alphaa вҖ” hento ruudukko-vihje, nГӨkyy ilman ettГӨ dominoi). Light-themelle erillinen override `[data-theme="light"] .heatmap-cell:not([class*="lvl-"]):not(.future) { border-color: rgba(15, 118, 110, 0.22); }` (--accent-dark, 22 % alpha вҖ” hieman vahvempi koska light bg vaatii kontrastia border-nГӨkyvyydelle). Lvl-luokitellut cellit saavat `border: 0` jotta tГӨytetty mint ei piirry kahdella reunalla. Future-cellit (jo himmennetyt 0.25 opacity) sГӨilyvГӨt ennallaan. **Valittiin Haara A** (subtile dashed-grid) eikГӨ Haara B (CTA korvaa heatmapin), koska Haara A sГӨilyttГӨГӨ 30 pГӨivГӨn ruudukon spatial-vihjeen myГ¶s ennen kuin kГӨyttГӨjГӨ on harjoitellut вҖ” kun ensimmГӨinen pГӨivГӨ syttyy, kГӨyttГӨjГӨ nГӨkee suoraan ettГӨ progressio piirtyy tГӨytettyihin slotteihin. **Skill applied:** `education/cognitive-load-analyser` (yksi visuaalinen elementti, ei tekstiГӨ eikГӨ CTA:ta heatmapin pГӨГӨllГӨ вҖ” jos kГӨyttГӨjГӨ tarvitsee CTA:n, `dash-day-cta`-banner nГӨkyy heti ylГӨpuolella), `design:design-system` (kГӨytetty olemassa olevia accent-tokeneita, ei uusia vГӨrejГӨ), `ui-ux-pro-max` (kontrasti dashed-borderille lГӨpinГӨkyvГӨllГӨ taustalla on tarkoituksellisesti pre-AA вҖ” empty-state ei kommunikoi semanttista sisГӨltГ¶ГӨ, se on pelkkГӨ spatial-vihje, joten 4.5:1-vaatimus ei sovellu).
- **[2026-05-03 L-LIVE-AUDIT-P0] UPDATE 3 вҖ” `.btn--cta__meta` kontrastin luettavuus.** `css/components/button.css` rivit 192вҖ“202: poistettiin `opacity: 0.78` -sГӨГӨtГ¶ joka kompositoi mint-20:n (#CCFBF1) navy:lla (#111827) noin 7:1:ksi. TГӨyttГӨ mint-20:tГӨ jГӨГӨ siis 0.78:lla noin AA:n yli mutta visuaalisesti washed-out. Nyt opacity 1.0 вҶ’ tГӨysi #CCFBF1 #111827:lla on noin 13:1, kommentti dokumentoi miksi. SГӨilyttГӨГӨ brГӨndi-tunnelman (`.btn--cta__title` on `var(--bg)` = ~16:1, `.btn--cta__arrow` on `var(--accent)` = ~10.7:1) вҖ” meta jГӨГӨ edelleen visuaalisesti hieman pehmeГӨmmГӨksi kuin title koska mint vs off-white, mutta ei enГӨГӨ nГӨy "lГӨhes nГӨkymГӨttГ¶mГӨnГӨ" kuten audit-screenshotissa. **Ei uutta tokenia** вҖ” STANDARDS В§3 trivial extension. **Skill applied:** `design:accessibility-review` (WCAG-laskenta tehty kГӨsin: #CCFBF1 on RGB(204,251,241) вҶ’ relative luminance ~0.913, #111827 on RGB(17,24,39) вҶ’ relative luminance ~0.0119, contrast ratio = (0.913 + 0.05) / (0.0119 + 0.05) вүҲ 15.5:1; 0.78 opacity:n kanssa kompositoituu ~7:1 jonka audit havaitsi luettavuusongelmaksi). **Ei selectorimuutosta** вҖ” brief etsi `.dash-quick-review .meta` mutta DOM-rakenne kГӨyttГӨГӨ tosiasiassa `[data-cta-meta]`-attribuuttia .btn--cta:n sisГӨllГӨ (`js/screens/dash-cta.js renderDashboardCta()`), joten oikea selector on `.btn--cta__meta`. Sama sГӨГӨntГ¶ koskee mode-page-CTA:ita ja kaikkia muita `.btn--cta__meta`-instansseja вҶ’ kaikki saavat saman luettavuusparannuksen.
- **[2026-05-03 L-LIVE-AUDIT-P0] UPDATE 4 вҖ” Hash-routing-confirm + x-button palaa lГӨhde-sivulle.** `js/main.js` `maybeConfirmNavAway()` laajennettiin: aiempi `if (!ctx) return true` -aikainen ulospГӨГӨstГ¶ poistui, nyt ehto on `if (!EXERCISE_SCREENS.has(screenId)) return true` (sama joukko kuin vanha lessonScreens). Modaali-copy haarautuu `isLesson = !!ctx`-flagin mukaan: lesson-haara sГӨilyttГӨГӨ L-PLAN-5 UPDATE 3:n "Lopetetaanko oppitunti?"-otsikon + lesson-focus-stringin, standalone-haara kГӨyttГӨГӨ uutta "Lopetetaanko harjoitus? вҖ” Vastauksesi tГӨhГӨn asti tallentuvat, mutta keskenerГӨistГӨ sessiota ei voi jatkaa myГ¶hemmin." -copya per brief. Primary "Lopeta" (lesson) tai "Lopeta ja siirry" (standalone), secondary "Jatka oppituntia" tai "Jatka harjoitusta". Lesson-context-clear ajetaan vain jos ctx oli totta вҖ” standalone-sessiolle ei ole stateГӨ clearattavaksi. X-button-haara: uusi `exitToSource(fallbackMode)`-helpper joka (a) jos lessonContext on auki, вҶ’ `screen-dashboard` (lesson-exit-flow sГӨilyy), (b) muuten navigoi `state.mode`-kenttГӨГӨn (vocab/grammar/reading/writing) вҶ’ `navigateTo()` joka mappaa `screen-mode-${mode}`-screeniin. `btn-exit-exercise/btn-exit-gram/btn-exit-reading/btn-exit-reading-text` saavat omat fallbackit (vocab/grammar/reading/reading) jotta state.mode-puutteen vaikkapa cold loadissa ei ohjaa vГӨГӨrГӨГӨn paikkaan. Hashchange-listeneriin ei lisГӨtty confirm-prompttia: hashchange fires AFTER hash-muutos, joten cancellointi vaatisi hash-rollbackin joka rikkoisi browserin back/forward-historian. Sidebar-buttonit ovat `<button data-nav="...">` (ei `<a href>`), joten click-handler ehtii ennen hash-muutosta вҖ” confirm-prompt riittГӨГӨ sieltГӨ. **Skill applied:** `puheo-finnish-voice` (standalone-modal "Vastauksesi tГӨhГӨn asti tallentuvat" вҖ” agentic, ei "menetГӨt edistyksesi" -negatiivinen frame; "Jatka harjoitusta" matchaa "Jatka oppituntia" -aiempaa rytmiГӨ), `design:ux-copy` (1 virke body, primary-action-label kertoo seurausketjun "Lopeta ja siirry"), `education/self-efficacy-builder-sequence` (ei shameta keskeyttГӨmistГӨ, vain neutraali fakta sГӨilytysstrategiasta), `ui-ux-pro-max` (sama olemassa oleva confirmDialog-primitiivi вҶ’ focus-trap, Escape, aria-modal-toiminnallisuus tulee bundlettuna).
- **[2026-05-03 L-LIVE-AUDIT-P0] UPDATE 5 вҖ” `/api/config/public` 404 korjattu serverless-buildissa.** Live-audit havaitsi `GET /api/config/public` palauttaa 404 tuotannossa (Vercel-deploy) vaikka `routes/config.js` on olemassa ja `server.js` mounttaa sen rivillГӨ 142. Juurisyy: `api/index.js` (Vercel serverless entry) ei mounttaa `configRoutes`, `statusRoutes`, eikГӨ `/api/waitlist`-endpointtia вҖ” tiedosto unohdettiin synkata `server.js`:n kanssa kun config + status + waitlist lisГӨttiin. Korjaus: importoidaan `configRoutes`, `statusRoutes`, `waitlistLimiter` ja `supabase` `api/index.js`:ssГӨ; mountataan `/api/config`, `/api/dev`, `/api/status` (sama dual-mount-kuvio kuin server.js:llГӨ вҖ” config-router palvelee sekГӨ `/public` GET:n ettГӨ `/grant-pro` POST:n) ja kopioidaan `/api/waitlist`-handler verbatim. Frontend `js/screens/writing.js hydrateConfig()` (rivi 207) saa nyt 200-vastauksen, `window.__WAITLIST_MODE` + `window.__DEV_PRO_ENABLED` hydratoituvat oikein, dev-tilin "Flip to Pro"-nappi alkaa renderГ¶ityГӨ testitileillГӨ myГ¶s tuotannossa. **Ei skill-overheadia** вҖ” chore/infra-fix, ei kГӨyttГӨjГӨlle nГӨkyvГӨГӨ copyГӨ eikГӨ UI-elementtiГӨ. Verifiointi: `node --check api/index.js` clean, `node --check routes/exam.js` clean (UPDATE 1:n discard-endpoint), `npm test` 1067/1067 вң“ (ei muutoksia testituloksissa вҖ” config-route ei ollut testattu erikseen).
- **[2026-05-03 L-LIVE-AUDIT-P0] verification.** `node --check` clean kaikilla 4 muokatulla JS-tiedostolla (`api/index.js`, `routes/exam.js`, `js/main.js`, `js/screens/fullExam.js`). `npm test` вҶ’ **1 067 testiГӨ passissa** (tГӨysi vihreГӨ, ei regressioita L-PLAN-8 baselinen jГӨlkeen). SW `CACHE_VERSION` v110 вҶ’ v111 koska `js/main.js`, `js/screens/fullExam.js` ja `css/components/dashboard.css` ovat STATIC_ASSETS-listalla (button.css ei ollut listalla pre-existing вҖ” ei lisГӨtty tГӨssГӨ loopissa, koska se vaatisi oman audit-passin "mitkГӨ CSS-tiedostot pitГӨisi cachata" -kysymyksen ratkomiseen). Manuaalitesti tuotannossa Vercel-deployn jГӨlkeen on kГӨyttГӨjГӨn tehtГӨvГӨ вҖ” agent-loop ei voi ajaa Pro-tunnuksin live-flowta ilman browser-MCP:tГӨ. **Deferred:** Playwright E2E `tests/e2e/exam-resume.spec.js` ja `tests/e2e/exit-active-exercise.spec.js` (CI-workflow on `workflow_dispatch`-gated commitin d3f5ca5 jГӨlkeen API-secrets-puutteen vuoksi вҖ” E2E-spekit kirjoitetaan kun secrets aukenevat). axe-core sweep + design:design-critique-passi muutetuista screeneistГӨ @ 1440 + 375 deferattu samasta syystГӨ (Playwright-stack riippuvainen). Pre-existing modal-primitiivi `confirmDialog` on jo a11y-clean (L-PLAN-8 axe-sweep clean, focus-trap/Escape/aria-modal kaikki paikoillaan), ja UPDATE 1:n inline-modaali kГӨyttГӨГӨ samaa CSS:ГӨГӨ + samaa fokus-trap-logiikkaa, joten regressiota ei odoteta.

## L-LIVE-AUDIT-P1 вҖ” visuaaliset polish-fixit dashboardiin + harjoitusscreeneihin (2026-05-03)

**Scope: 7 P1-tason visuaalista lГ¶ydГ¶stГӨ `AUDIT_LIVE_DASHBOARD.md`:stГӨ вҖ” kГӨyttГӨjГӨn vahvistettu lopputavoite "Dashboard tuntuu yhtГӨ viimeistellyltГӨ kuin Linear tai Vercel; tehtГӨvГӨsivut nГӨyttГӨvГӨt opetussisГӨllГ¶ltГӨ, eivГӨt terminaalilta; brand-vГӨrit eivГӨt klashaa keskenГӨГӨn." Ei toiminnallisuuden muutoksia, ei uusia API:ja. UPDATE 8 on selvitys + pГӨГӨtГ¶sehdotus, ei koodimuutos.**

- **[2026-05-03 L-LIVE-AUDIT-P1] UPDATE 1 вҖ” `dash-tutor` selkeГӨmpi kortti.** `css/components/dashboard.css` rivit 884вҖ“905: `.dash-tutor` siirtyi `var(--surface)` + `padding: 16px 20px` вҶ’ `var(--surface-2)` + `padding: 24px` + `border-radius: var(--r-lg, 16px)` + `margin: 20px auto 24px`. Border-left kavennettu 3 px вҶ’ 2 px (subtle accent cue, ei alert-laatikko-vibes). Mobile @ вүӨ768 px вҶ’ 20 px padding + 16 px y-margin. `.dash-tutor__msg` 17 px вҶ’ 15 px, vГӨri `--ink` вҶ’ `--ink-soft` (sub-tutor body kuten VercelillГӨ, line-height pidetГӨГӨn 1.6). Brief:n proposed-CSS implementoitu screen-template-tokeneilla вҖ” `--r-lg`, `--space-6`/`--space-4`-spacing puhuttelee `puheo-screen-template`-skill-spec:iГӨ. **Skill applied:** `puheo-screen-template` (token-pohjat: `--surface-2`, `--r-lg`), `ui-ux-pro-max` (line-height вүҘ 1.55 leipГӨtekstille, 24 px padding kortin breath-alueena), `design:design-system` (sГӨilytetty olemassa olevat tokenit, ei uusia). 21st.dev sourcing: trivial extension olemassa olevasta L-PLAN-3 kortti-primitiivistГӨ (STANDARDS В§3 "trivial extension" -poikkeus) вҖ” sama elementti, kovennettu spacing + restrained accent.
- **[2026-05-03 L-LIVE-AUDIT-P1] UPDATE 2 вҖ” Level-progress-card korvaa paljaan "B вҶ’ C" -laatikon.** `js/screens/adaptive.js renderAdaptiveCard()` `pending`-haara muotoiltu uudelleen: aiempi `<div>${data.currentLevel} вҶ’ ${data.nextLevel}</div>` + 4 raakaa `progressRow`:ta on nyt `<p class="lpc-eyebrow">Tasosi edistyminen</p>` + `<h3 class="lpc-title">Matka tasolle ${nextLevel}</h3>` + `<p class="lpc-hint">Kun tГӨytГӨt kaikki neljГӨ tavoitetta, sinut pГӨivitetГӨГӨn ${nextLevel}-tasolle.</p>` + 2-sarakkeinen `.lpc-grid` (1-sarakkeinen вүӨ640 px), neljГӨ `.lpc-metric`-riviГӨ (label + tabular-num arvo + 4 px progress-palkki), absoluuttisesti positioitu `.lpc-badge` (currentLevel вҶ’ nextLevel) oikeassa ylГӨkulmassa (kollabautuu inline-pilliksi вүӨ480 px). `progressRow()`-helper kirjoitettu uudelleen: `aria-valuenow`/`aria-valuemin`/`aria-valuemax` + `aria-label`, `is-done`-luokka kun `current >= target` (palkki + numero `--success`). Light-theme override `--accent-dark`-pohjalla badge + bar-fill -elementeille AA-kontrastin vuoksi. **Skill applied:** `puheo-screen-template` (eyebrow + h3 + hint hierarchy = screen-template-spec), `puheo-finnish-voice` (suomalainen otsikointi, "tasolle C" ei "C-tasolle" kohti agentticempaa kieltГӨ), `education/self-efficacy-builder-sequence` (deklaratiivinen, ei shame-frame), `ui-ux-pro-max` (`role="progressbar"` + label, focus-states perittyГӨ). **21st.dev sourcing:** [21st.dev/s/progress-card](https://21st.dev/s/progress-card) (port stats/goal-tracker -patternista, restrained dark variant вҖ” eyebrow + h3 + grid of metric rows + corner badge).

Bar-elementti oli jo paikallaan; muutos on puhdas readability-fix. CSS `css/components/dashboard.css` `.dash-readiness-headline` + `.dash-readiness-pct` + `.dash-readiness-track` lisГӨtty olemassa olevan `.dash-readiness-summary`-sГӨГӨnnГ¶n perГӨГӨn, ei uusia tokeneita. **Skill applied:** `education/cognitive-load-analyser` (poistettu yksi visuaalinen elementti вҖ” legend вҖ” jonka kognitiivinen hinta oli korkeampi kuin info-arvo), `puheo-finnish-voice` (pilkku, em-dash вҶ’ keskipiste), `puheo-screen-template` (eyebrow + dominant numero + bar вҖ” sama hierarkia kuin grader-card landing-pagessa). **21st.dev sourcing:** [21st.dev/s/horizontal-bar](https://21st.dev/s/horizontal-bar) вҖ” sГӨilytetty olemassa oleva `.dash-wp-row`-rakenne joka jo seurasi tГӨtГӨ patternia, lisГӨtty pienet readability-fixit Finnish-locale + trendin valikoiva renderГ¶inti.
